jane goodall helps humans and animals live together	珍的善良幫助人類和動物一起生活在一起 , 珍妮•布爾 , 能協助人類和動物一起生活 。
good afternoon , good evening , whatever .	晚安 , 晚安 , 不管如何 。
we can go , jambo , guten abend , bonsoir , but we can also ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh , ooh .	我們可以去 , 詹姆斯 , 阿布蘭 , 鮑林 , 但我們也能ooh , ooh , oh , oh , oh , oh , oh , oh , oh , oh 。
that is the call that chimpanzees make before they go to sleep in the evening .	這就是黑猩猩在晚上睡前的電話 。
you hear it going from one side of the valley to the other , from one group of nests to the next .	你聽到它來自谷歌的一面 , 從一組巢穴到下一個 。
and i want to pick up with my talk this evening from where zeray left off yesterday .	我想要從昨天離開那天晚上拿起我的演講 。
he was talking about this amazing , threeyearold australopithecine child , selam .	他在談論這個驚人的 , 三歲的澳洲人兒童 , 塞拉姆 。
and we've also been hearing about the history , the family tree , of mankind through dna genetic profiling .	我們也聽到了歷史 , 家庭樹 , 透過dna基因獲利的人類 。
and it was a paleontologist , the late louis leakey , who actually set me on the path for studying chimpanzees .	那是一名古生物學家 , 最近的路易斯•利基 , 他讓我在研究黑猩猩的路上 。
and it was pretty extraordinary , way back then .	當時它很不可思議 , 回到那時 。
it's kind of commonplace now , but his argument was because he'd been searching for the fossilized remains of early humans in africa .	這有點常見 , 但他的論點是 , 因為他一直在尋找非洲早期人類的化石 。
and you can tell an awful lot about what those beings looked like from the fossils , from the shape of the muscle attachments , something about the way they lived from the various artifacts found with them .	你可以告訴大家 , 那些來自化石的樣子 , 來自肌肉的形狀 , 從肌肉的形狀 , 到他們從各種不同的人工發現的方式 。
but what about how they behaved ? that's what he wanted to know .	但他們是怎麼樣的 ? 這是他想知道的 。
and of course , behavior doesn't fossilize .	當然 , 行為不會化石化 。
he argued and it's now a fairly common theory that if we found behavior patterns similar or the same in our closest living relatives , the great apes , and humans today , then maybe those behaviors were present in the apelike , humanlike ancestor some seven million years ago .	他主張了 , 現在是一個很常見的理論 , 如果我們發現行為模式和我們近親親的親戚相似 , 人類 , 或許這些行為會出現在同一百七百萬年前 , 人類的祖先 。
and therefore , perhaps we had brought those characteristics with us from that ancient , ancient past .	因此 , 也許我們把這些特質帶給我們 , 從古老、古老的過去 。
well , if you look in textbooks today that deal with human evolution , you very often find people speculating about how early humans may have behaved , based on the behavior of chimpanzees .	嗯 , 如果你今天看教科書來處理人類進化 , 你通常會發現人們在測量早期人類的行為 , 可能是基於黑猩猩的行為 。
they are more like us than any other living creature , and we've heard about that during this ted conference .	他們比其他生物更像我們 , 我們在ted會議中聽過這個 。
so it remains for me to comment on the ways in which chimpanzees are so like us , in certain aspects of their behavior .	所以 , 它留給我說 , 黑猩猩和我們相似 , 在某些方面 , 牠們的行為的某些方面 。
every chimpanzee has his or her own personality .	每個黑猩猩都有他或自己的個人性 。
of course , i gave them names . they can live to be 60 years or more , although we think most of them probably don't make it to 60 in the wild .	當然 , 我給他們名字 , 他們可以活60年或更久 , 雖然我們認為大部分人可能不會在野生裡達到60歲 。
mr . wurzel . the female has her first baby when she's 11 or 12 .	沃爾茲 , 雌性在11或12歲時 , 她是第一個嬰兒 。
thereafter , she has one baby only every five or six years , a long period of childhood dependency when the child is nursing , sleeping with the mother at night , and riding on her back .	在那裡 , 她每五到六年 , 只有一個嬰兒 , 長期的兒童依賴 , 當孩子們在睡眠 , 晚上睡著 , 和她一起騎回來 。
and we believe that this long period of childhood is important for chimpanzees , just as it is for us , in relation to learning .	我們相信 , 這種長期的童年對黑猩猩來說很重要 , 就像是為了我們 , 學習的關係 。
as the brain becomes ever more complex during evolution in different forms of animals , so we find that learning plays an ever more important role in an individual's life history .	當大腦在不同類型的動物演化過程中變得更複雜 , 所以我們發現 , 學習在個人生命歷史中扮演著更重要的角色 。
and young chimpanzees spend a lot of time watching what their elders do .	年輕的黑猩猩花了很多時間觀察他們的老年人做些什麼 。
we know now that they're capable of imitating behaviors that they see .	我們現在知道 , 他們能夠模仿他們所看到的行為 。
and we believe that it's in this way that the different toolusing behaviors that have now been seen in all the different chimpanzee populations studied in africa how these are passed from one generation to the next , through observation , imitation and practice , so that we can describe these toolusing behaviors as primitive culture .	我們相信 , 這種方式是不同的工具行為 , 目前在非洲各式各樣的黑猩猩族群都被研究 , 如何從一個世代傳遞到下一代 , 通過觀察 , 模仿和練習 , 這樣我們就能描述這些細微的行為 , 成為原始文化 。
chimpanzees don't have a spoken language . we've talked about that .	黑猩猩沒有語言 , 我們談過這一點 。
they do have a very rich repertoire of postures and gestures , many of which are similar , or even identical , to ours and formed in the same context . greeting chimpanzees embracing .	他們的確有非常豐富的姿勢和姿勢 , 許多都是相似的 , 甚至相同的 , 在同一個情況下 , 希臘黑猩猩會擁抱 。
they also kiss , hold hands , pat one another on the back .	他們也吻了 , 握住手 , 另一隻手 。
and they swagger and they throw rocks .	牠們會游泳 , 丟出岩石 。
in chimpanzee society , we find many , many examples of compassion , precursors to love and true altruism .	在黑猩猩社會中 , 我們發現許多許多同情的例子 , 像是愛和真實的利他主義 。
unfortunately , they , like us , have a dark side to their nature .	不幸的是 , 他們跟我們一樣 , 有一面黑暗的面向 。
they're capable of extreme brutality , even a kind of primitive war .	他們有能力極端的殘酷性 , 甚至是一種原始的戰爭 。
and these really aggressive behaviors , for the most part , are directed against individuals of the neighboring social group .	這些真的很具侵略性的行為 , 最多部分是對鄰近社會團體的個體 。
they are very territorially aggressive .	它們是非常嚴格的侵略性 。
chimpanzees , i believe , more than any other living creature , have helped us to understand that , after all , there is no sharp line between humans and the rest of the animal kingdom .	我相信 , 黑猩猩 , 我相信 , 比任何其他生物還能幫助我們了解 , 畢竟 , 人類和其他動物王國之間沒有鯊魚線 。
it's a very blurry line , and it's getting more blurry all the time as we make even more observations .	這是一條非常模糊的線 , 隨著我們做出更多觀察時 , 就會變得越來越模糊 。
the study that i began in 1960 is still continuing to this day .	我從1960年開始的研究仍然持續到今日 。
and these chimpanzees , living their complex social lives in the wild , have helped more than anything else to make us realize we are part of , and not separated from , the amazing animals with whom we share the planet .	而這些黑猩猩 , 活在野生的複雜社會生活中 , 比其他東西更有幫助讓我們了解我們是其中一部分 , 而不是我們共享地球的神奇動物 。
so it's pretty sad to find that chimpanzees , like so many other creatures around the world , are losing their habitats .	所以很難找到黑猩猩 , 就像世界上許多其他生物一樣 , 都失去了棲息地 。
this is just one photograph from the air , and it shows you the forested highlands of gombe .	這只是從空氣中拍攝的照片 , 它顯示了你在大西的森林高地 。
and it was when i flew over the whole area , about 16 years ago , and realized that outside the park , this forest , which in 1960 had stretched almost unbroken along the eastern shore of lake tanganyika , which is where the tiny , 30squaremile gombe national park lies , that a question came to my mind .	當時我飛過整個區域 , 大約16年前 , 我發現 , 在公園外面 , 森林在1960年代 , 幾乎沒有破壞 , 湖泊的海岸 , 也就是小型的三十平方公尺的公園 , 一個問題來到我腦海中 。
" how can we even try to save these famous chimpanzees , when the people living around the national park are struggling to survive ? "	「 我們要如何拯救這些有名的黑猩猩 , 當國家公園裡的人在掙扎存活下來時 ? 」
more people are living there than the land could possibly support .	更多人住在那裏 , 比陸地還能支持 。
the numbers increased by refugees pouring in from burundi and over the lake from congo .	難民的數量增加 , 來自緬甸 , 和剛果湖泊的湖泊 。
and very poor people they couldn't afford to buy food from elsewhere .	非常貧窮的人 , 他們無法從其他地方買食物 。
this led to a program , which we call tacare .	這導致了一項計畫 , 我們稱之為 「 計劃 」 。
it's a very holistic way of improving the lives of the people living in the villages around the park .	這是一種非常嚴格的改善人們生活在村莊裡的生活方式 。
it started small with 12 villages . it's now in 24 .	它從12個村落開始 , 現在已經在24年了 。
there isn't time to go into it , but it's including things like tree nurseries , methods of farming most suitable to this now very degraded , almost desertlike land up in these mountains .	沒有時候要走進去 , 但它包含了像樹管的樣子 , 農場最適合的農場 , 幾乎是沙漠在這些山脈上降落 。
ways of controlling , preventing soil erosion .	控制方式 , 防止土壤排放 。
ways of reclaiming overused farmland , so that within two years they can again be productive .	再次重建農地的方法 , 所以在兩年內 , 他們能再次成為生產力 。
working to help the villagers obtain fresh water from wells .	努力協助村民從好處取得淡水 。
perhaps build some schoolrooms .	也許建造一些學校 。
most important of all , i believe , is working with small groups of women , providing them with opportunities for microcredit loans .	最重要的是 , 我相信 , 與少數女性合作 , 提供他們對微型credit貸款的機會 。
and we've got , as is the case around the world , about 95 percent of all loans returned .	我們得到了 , 如同全世界的情況 , 大約百分之九十五的貸款回來 。
empowering women , working with education , providing scholarships for girls so they can finish secondary school , in the clear understanding that , all around the world , as women's education improves , family size drops .	賦予女性 , 和教育合作 , 為女孩提供獎學金 , 讓他們能夠完成第二級學校 , 清楚地了解到全世界各地 , 女性的教育改善 , 家庭大小 。
we provide information about family planning and about hiv/aids .	我們提供關於家庭規劃和愛滋病的資訊 。
and as a result of this program , something's happening for conservation .	由於這個計畫的結果 , 有些事情正在發生 。
what's happening for conservation is that the farmers living in these 24 villages , instead of looking on us as a bunch of white people coming to study a whole bunch of monkeys and by the way , many of the staff are now tanzanian but when we began the tacare program , it was a tanzanian team going into the villages .	保育的情況是 , 農夫生活在24個村莊裡 , 而不是把我們當作一群白人來研究一堆猴子 , 還有 , 很多人現在是坦尚尼亞 , 但當我們開始計劃時 , 它是坦尚尼亞的團隊 。
it was a tanzanian team talking to the villagers , asking what they were interested in .	這是一個坦尚尼亞的團隊和村民談話 , 問他們對他們的興趣是什麼 。
were they interested in conservation ? absolutely not .	他們對保育有興趣嗎 ? 絕對不是 。
they were interested in health ; they were interested in education .	他們對健康有興趣 , 他們對教育有興趣 。
and as time went on , and as their situation began to improve , they began to understand ever more about the need for conservation .	隨著時間進步 , 隨著他們的情況開始改善 , 他們開始更了解保育需要的需求 。
they began to understand that as the upper levels of the hills were denuded of trees , so you've got this terrible soil erosion and mudslides .	他們開始了解 , 身為山丘的上層層面 , 所以你有很糟糕的土壤排放和泥土 。
today , we are developing what we call the greater gombe ecosystem .	現今 , 我們正在開發出我們所謂的 「 更偉大的高爾蒙生態系統 」 。
this is an area way outside the national park , stretching out into all these very degraded lands .	這是國家公園外的一個地方 , 伸出這些非常乾燥的土地 。
and as these villages have a better standard of life , they are actually agreeing to put between 10 percent and 20 percent of their land in the highlands aside , so that once again , as the trees grow back , the chimpanzees will have leafy corridors through which they can travel to interact as they must for genetic viability with other remnant groups outside the national park .	隨著這些村莊有更好的生命標準 , 他們其實同意將百分之十到二十的土地的土地 , 再一次 , 當樹木長回來時 , 黑猩猩會透過他們能與其他國家公園的基因互動 。
so tacare is a success .	所以tacare是成功的 。
we're replicating it in other parts of africa , around other wilderness areas which are faced with extreme population pressure .	我們在非洲其他地方複製它 , 在其他地方 , 和其他荒野區域面臨極端的人口壓力 。
the problems in africa , however , as we've been discussing for the whole of these first couple of days of ted , are major problems .	然而 , 非洲的問題 , 隨著我們在討論ted的前幾天 , ted是主要的問題 。
there is a great deal of poverty .	有很多貧窮 。
and when you get large numbers of people living in land that is not that fertile , particularly when you cut down trees , and you leave the soil open to the wind for erosion , as desperate populations cut down more and more trees , so that they can try and grow food for themselves and their families , what's going to happen ? something's got to give .	當你有大量的人住在土地裡 , 尤其是你砍伐樹 , 離開土壤 , 把土壤砍掉 , 把更多的樹木砍掉 , 所以他們可以為自己種植食物 , 什麼會發生 ?
and the other problems in not only africa , but the rest of the developing world and , indeed , everywhere what are we doing to our planet ?	另外一個問題不只是非洲 , 而是其他發展中國家的其他問題 , 確實 , 我們在地球上所做的事 ?
you know , the famous scientist , e . o . wilson said that if every person on this planet attains the standard of living of the average european or american , we need three new planets .	你知道 , 一位有名的科學家 , e.o.o.wilson說如果地球上的每個人都活在歐洲或美國 , 我們需要三個新的行星 。
today , they are saying four . but we don't have them . we've got one .	今天 , 他們說了四個 , 但我們沒有他們 。 我們有一個 。
and what's happened ? i mean , the question here is , here we are , arguably the most intelligent being that's ever walked planet earth , with this extraordinary brain , capable of the kind of technology that is so well illustrated by these ted conferences , and yet we're destroying the only home we have .	發生了什麼事 ? 我的意思是 , 這裡的問題是 , 我們最有智慧的 , 是地球上最有智慧的人類 , 這種非凡的大腦 , 能夠被ted會議所描繪出的技術 , 但我們卻摧毀了我們唯一的家 。
the indigenous people around the world , before they made a major decision , used to sit around and ask themselves , " how does this decision affect our people seven generations ahead ? "	世界各地的原住民 , 在他們做了一個重大決定之前 , 以前 , 常常會問自己: 「 這決定如何影響我們的七代人 ? 」
today , major decisions and i'm not particularly talking about africa here , but the developed world major decisions involving millions of dollars , and millions of people , are often based on , " how will this affect the next shareholders' meeting ? "	今天 , 主要的決策 , 我不特別在談論非洲 , 但開發中國家的主要決策是數百萬美金 , 而數百萬人通常是基於 「 這會如何影響下一個共享者的會議 ? 」
and these decisions affect africa .	這些決策會影響非洲 。
as i began traveling around africa talking about the problems faced by chimpanzees and their vanishing forests , i realized more and more how so many of africa's problems could be laid at the door of previous colonial exploitation .	當我開始在非洲各地探討黑猩猩和他們消失的森林時 , 我了解到 , 越來越多非洲的問題 , 可能在以前的殖民部門 。
so i began traveling outside africa , talking in europe , talking in the united states , going to asia .	所以 , 我開始在非洲旅行 , 在歐洲談話 , 在美國 , 去亞洲 。
and everywhere there were these terrible problems .	每個地方都有這些可怕的問題 。
and you know the kind i'm talking about . i'm talking about pollution .	各位知道我在說的這種事 , 我談的是污染 。
the air that we breathe that often poisons us .	我們呼吸的空氣通常會引起我們 。
the earth is poisoning our foods .	地球是毒害我們的食物 。
the water water is perhaps one of the most crucial issues that we're going to face in this century and everywhere water is being polluted by agricultural , industrial and household chemicals that still are being sprayed around the world , seemingly with the inability to profit from past experience .	水可能是我們在這個世紀所面對的最關鍵問題之一 , 到處都是農業、工業和家庭化學物質 , 仍然被全世界散播出來 , 似乎是無法從過去經驗中獲利的 。
the mangroves are being cut down ; the effects of things like the tsunami get worse .	紅外線被切割 ; 像海嘯的影響會更糟 。
we've talked about the soil erosion .	我們談過土壤排放 。
we have the reckless burning of fossil fuels along with other greenhouse gasses , so called , leading to climate change .	我們有不可思議的化石燃料和其他溫室氣體 , 叫做 , 導致氣候變遷 。
finally , all around the world , people have begun to believe that there is something going on very wrong with our climate .	最後 , 世界各地 , 人們開始相信 , 我們的氣候發生了很大的錯誤 。
all around the world climates are mixed up .	世界各地的氣候都混合起來 。
and it's the poor people who are affected worse .	最貧窮的人會更糟糕 。
it's africa that already is affected .	非洲已經受到影響 。
in many parts of subsaharan africa , the droughts are so much worse .	在撒哈拉以南非洲的許多地區 , 乾旱非常糟糕 。
and when the rain does come , it so often leads to flooding and added distress , and the cycle of poverty and hunger and disease .	當雨林來臨時 , 通常會導致洪水、加熱 , 以及貧窮、飢餓和疾病的循環 。
and the numbers of people living in an area that the land cannot support , who are too poor to buy food , who can't move away because the whole land is degraded .	而住在一個地方的人數無法支援 , 他們太貧窮了 , 因為整個土地已經退化了 。
and so you get desertification creeping , creeping , creeping as the last of the trees are cut down .	所以 , 你會得到沙漠化 , 哭泣 , 直到最後一棵樹被砍掉 。
and this kind of thing is not just in africa . it's all over the world .	這種事情不僅在非洲 , 都在全世界 。
so it wasn't surprising to me that as i was traveling around the world i met so many young people who seemed to have lost hope .	所以這並不讓我驚訝的是 , 當我在世界各地旅行時 , 我遇到許多年輕人似乎失去了希望 。
we seem to have lost wisdom , the wisdom of the indigenous people .	我們似乎失去了智慧 , 原住民的智慧 。
i asked a question . " why ? "	我問了一個問題: 「 為什麼 ? 」
well , do you think there could be some kind of disconnect between this extraordinarily clever brain , the kind of brain that the ted technologies exemplify , and the human heart ? talking about it in the nonscientific term , in terms of love and compassion . is there some disconnect ?	嗯 , 你認為 , 可能有某種不可思議的大腦 , 這種關於ted科技的大腦 , 和人類的心臟擴大 , 談論它 , 在非科學方面 , 在愛和同情上 , 是否有某種不同嗎 ?
and these young people , when i talk to them , basically they were either depressed or apathetic , or bitter and angry . and they said more or less the same thing , " we feel this way because we feel you've compromised our future and there's nothing we can do about it . "	而這些年輕人 , 當我跟他們說話時 , 基本上他們是憂鬱或痛苦 , 或憤怒 。 他們說了更多或少的同一件事 , 因為我們覺得你對未來的貢獻 , 沒有任何我們能做的事 。 」
we have compromised their future .	我們已經承諾了他們的未來 。
i've got three little grandchildren , and every time i look at them and i think how we've harmed this beautiful planet since i was their age , i feel this desperation .	我有三個小孫子 , 每次我看著他們 , 我想我們如何傷害這個美麗的星球 , 我覺得這個絕望 。
and that led to this program we call roots and shoots , which began right here in tanzania and has now spread to 97 countries around the world .	結果導致了這個計畫 , 我們稱之為根和射擊 , 開始在坦尚尼亞 , 現在已經擴散到全世界的97個國家 。
it's symbolic . roots make a firm foundation .	它是象徵性的 。 根源製造了一間公司基金會 。
shoots seem tiny ; to reach the sun they can break through a brick wall .	射擊似乎很小 , 到達太陽 , 可以穿過一面磚牆 。
see the brick wall as all these problems we've inflicted on the planet , environmental and social . it's a message of hope .	把磚牆看成我們在地球上所帶來的所有問題 , 環境和社交 。 這是希望的訊息 。
hundreds and thousands of young people around the world can break through and can make this a better world for all living things .	全世界有數以千計的年輕人可以打破 , 讓這世界變得更好 。
the most important message of roots and shoots: every single one of us makes a difference , every single day .	最重要的訊息是根和槍擊:我們每一個人都造成了差異 , 每一天 。
we have a choice . every one of us in this room , we have a choice as to what kind of difference we want to make .	我們有選擇 。 在這間房間裡的每一個人 , 我們都有選擇 , 我們想要做些什麼樣的差異 。
the very poor have no choice . it's up to us to change things so that the poor have choice as well .	窮人沒有選擇 , 我們就要改變事情 , 讓窮人有選擇 。
the roots and shoots groups all choose three projects .	根和槍擊團體都選擇了三項計畫 。
it depends on how old they are , and which country , whether they're in a city or rural , as to what kinds of projects .	它依賴了多少年紀 , 哪個國家 , 不論是城市或鄉村 , 為何種項目 。
but basically , we have programs now from preschool right through university , with more and more adults starting their own roots and shoots groups .	但基本上 , 我們已經從學院學院開始了 , 有更多成年人開始自己的根和槍擊團體 。
and every group chooses , between them , three different kinds of project to make this a better world , recognizing that all these different problems are interconnected and impinge on each other .	每個團體選擇 , 三個不同的項目 , 讓這個世界變得更好 , 意識到 , 所有這些不同的問題都互相連結 , 連接彼此 。
so one of their projects will be to help their own human community .	所以 , 其中一個計畫將會協助自己的人類社群 。
and then , if they're able , they may raise money to help communities in other parts of the world .	然後 , 如果他們能做到 , 他們可能會在世界上其他地方提高錢 , 來協助社區 。
one of their projects will be to help animals not just wildlife , domestic animals as well .	其中一個計畫 , 協助動物不僅僅是野生動物 , 家庭動物也是 。
and one of their projects will be to help the environment that we all share .	其中一個計畫將會幫助我們共享的環境 。
and woven throughout all of this is a message of learning to live in peace and harmony within ourselves , in our families , in our communities , between nations , between cultures , between religions and between us and the natural world .	所有這一切 , 是學習生活在和平和諧之中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的社區之間 , 在文化之間 , 文化和我們之間的宗教和自然世界之間 。
we need the natural world . we cannot go on destroying it at the rate we are .	我們需要自然的世界 , 我們不能在我們所處的速度下摧毀它 。
we not do have more than this one planet .	我們沒有超過這個星球 。
just picking one or two of the projects right here in africa that the roots and shoots groups are doing , one or two projects only in tanzania , in uganda , kenya , south africa , congobrazzaville , sierra leone , cameroon and other groups . and as i say , it's in 97 countries around the world .	在非洲 , 選一或兩項專案計畫 , 非洲的根和槍擊團體都在做 , 一、兩項專案 , 在烏干達 , 南非 , 南非 , 剛果的黎巴嫩 , 相機和其他組織 。 我說 , 在全世界97個國家 。
of course , they're planting trees . they're growing organic vegetables .	當然 , 它們正在種植樹 , 它們在種植有機蔬菜 。
they're working in the refugee camps , with chickens and selling the eggs for a little amount of money , or just using them to feed their families , and feeling a sense of pride and empowerment , because they're no longer helpless and depending on others with their vegetables and their chickens .	他們在難民營工作 , 有雞 , 賣蛋 , 或用小錢來餵養他們的家人 , 感受到自己是無助的 , 因為他們不再有幫助 , 依賴其他蔬菜和雞 。
it's being used in uganda to give some psychological help to exchild soldiers .	它被用在烏干達 , 給予一些心理上的幫助 , 來證明士兵 。
doing projects like this is bringing them out of themselves .	做像這樣的計畫 , 就是把他們從自己中取出來 。
once again , they're useful members of society .	再一次 , 他們是社會上有用的成員 。
we have this program in prisons as well .	我們在監獄裡也有這個計畫 。
so , there's no time for more roots and shoots now .	所以 , 現在沒有更多的根和射擊時間 。
but oh , they're also working on hiv/aids .	但 , 喔 , 他們也在研究愛滋病 ,
that's a very important component of roots and shoots , with older kids talking to younger ones .	這是個非常重要的根源和槍擊 , 長大的孩子和年輕的孩子談話 。
and unwanted pregnancies and things like that , which young people listen to better from other youth , rather than adults .	沒有預防的懷孕和類似的事情 , 年輕人會傾聽其他年輕人 , 而不是成人 。
hope . that's the question i get asked as i'm going around the world: " jane , you've seen so many terrible things , you've seen your chimpanzees decrease in number from about one million , at the turn of the century , to no more than 150 , 000 now , and the same with so many other animals .	希望 。 這是我在世界各地問的問題: 「 珍 , 你見過這麼多可怕的事情 , 你看到你的黑猩猩從一個世紀開始 , 開始 , 沒有超過150萬隻 , 和其他其他動物一樣 。
forests disappearing , deserts where once there was forest .	森林消失 , 沙漠一旦有森林 。
do you really have hope ? " well , yes .	你真的有希望嗎 ? " 嗯 , 是的 。
you can't come to a conference like ted and not have hope , can you ?	你不能來到ted的研討會 , 沒有希望 , 可以嗎 ?
and of course , there's hope . one is this amazing human brain .	當然 , 有希望 。 一個是令人驚嘆的人類腦 。
and i mean , think of the technologies .	我的意思是 , 想想科技 。
and i've just been so thrilled , finally , to come to people talking about compost latrines .	最後 , 我一直很興奮 , 終於 , 來到人們談的是創作洛杉磯 。
it's one of my hobbyhorses .	這是我最討厭的其中之一 。
we just flush all this water down the lavatory , it's terrible .	我們只是把這些水流下 , 很可怕 。
and then talking about renewable energy desperately important .	再來談談再生能源的重要性 。
do we care about the planet for our children ?	我們是否在乎我們的孩子嗎 ?
how many of us have children or grandchildren , nieces , nephews ?	有多少人有孩子或孫子 , 姪女 , 新人 ?
do we care about their future ?	我們是否在乎他們的未來嗎 ?
and if we care about their future , we , as the elite around the world , we can do something about it . we can make choices as to how we live each day .	如果我們關心他們的未來 , 我們 , 身為全世界的菁英 , 我們能做點什麼 。 我們可以把選擇做為我們每天的生活 。
what we buy . what we wear .	我們買了什麼 , 穿什麼衣服 。
and choose to make these choices with the question , how will this affect the environment around me ?	選擇讓這些選擇和問題做出選擇 , 如何影響我周遭的環境 ?
how will it affect the life of my child when he or she grows up ?	當他長大後 , 它會如何影響我的孩子的生命 ?
or my grandchild , or whatever it is .	或是我的孫子 , 或任何東西 。
so the human brain , coupled with the human heart , and we join hands around the world .	所以 , 人類的大腦 , 與人類的心 , 我們和世界各地的手合作 。
and that's what ted is helping so well with , and google who help us , and esri are helping us with mapping in gombe national park .	ted是如此的幫助 , 谷歌幫助我們 , esri正在幫助我們 , esri正在幫我們繪製全國公園 。
all of these technologies we can use .	所有我們能使用的技術 。
now let's link them , and it's beginning to happen , isn't it ?	咱們來連結它們 , 開始發生 , 不是嗎 ?
you've heard about it this afternoon . it's beginning to happen .	你已經聽過這個下午 , 開始發生 。
this change , this change . to see change that we must have if we care about the future .	這個改變 , 看看我們是否在乎未來的改變 。
and the next reason for hope nature is amazingly resilient .	希望大自然的下一個理由很了不起 。
you can take an area that's absolutely destroyed , with time and perhaps some help it can regenerate .	你可以拿一個絕對摧毀的區域 , 有時間 , 或許有些幫助它能再生 。
and an example is the tacare program .	一個例子是 「 計劃計畫 」 。
i told you , where a seemingly dead tree stump if you stop hacking them for firewood , which you don't need to because you have wood lots , then in five years you can have a 30foot tree .	我告訴你們 , 似乎是死的樹木 , 如果你停止把它們駭進火災 , 你不需要 , 因為你有木材 , 五年後 , 你可以有30英尺的樹木 。
and animals , almost on the brink of extinction , can be given a second chance . that's my next book .	動物 , 幾乎在滅絕的橋上 , 可能有第二次機會 。 這是我的下一本書 。
it's inspiring . and it brings me to my last category of hope , and we've heard about this so much in the last two days: this indomitable human spirit . this determination of people , the resilience of the human spirit , so that people who you would think would be battered by poverty , or disease , or whatever , can pull themselves up out of it , sometimes with a helping hand , and take their part in society , and take their part in changing the world .	很鼓舞人心 , 讓我帶到我最後的希望 , 我們在過去兩天聽過這一點:這種無限的人類精神 。 人類的靈魂 , 所以你認為你會被貧窮或疾病 , 或疾病 , 不管如何 , 可以把自己推出去 , 有時候 , 在社會改變世界 。
and just to think of one or two people out of africa who are just really inspiring .	想一下 , 非洲有一或兩個人 , 他們真的很鼓舞人心 。
we could make a very long list , but obviously nelson mandela , emerging from 17 years of hard physical labor , 23 years of imprisonment , with this amazing ability to forgive , so that he could lead his nation out the evil regime of apartheid without a bloodbath .	我們能做出非常長的清單 , 但顯然是nelson曼德拉 , 從17年的硬體勞動力 , 出現了23年的監禁 , 讓他能引領他國家的種族隔離 , 沒有血浴 。
ken sarowiwa , in nigeria , who took on the giant oil companies , and although people around the world tried their best , was executed .	在奈及利亞 , 肯•薩瓦 , 他在巨大的石油公司 , 雖然世界各地的人們都試過最好的 , 被拯救了 。
people like this are so inspirational .	像這樣的人非常靈感 。
people like this are the role models we need for young africans .	像這樣的人 , 是我們對年輕非洲人所需要的角色模式 。
and we need some environmental role models as well , and i've been hearing some of them today .	我們也需要一些環保的模型 , 我今天聽到了其中一些 。
so i'm really grateful for this opportunity to share this message again , with everyone at ted .	所以 , 我非常感謝這個機會再次分享這個訊息 , 和ted的所有人 。
and i hope that some of us can get together and talk about some of these things , especially the roots and shoots program .	我希望有些人可以一起討論這些事情 , 尤其是根和射擊計畫 。
and just a last word on that the young woman who's running this entire conference center , i met her today .	最後一個字是 , 年輕的女士在進行這整個會議中心 , 我今天見到她 。
she came up so excited , with her certificate . she was [in] roots and shoots .	她很興奮 , 和她的證據很興奮 。 她是 「 根和槍擊 」 。
she was in the leadership in dar es salaam .	她在達爾斯薩拉克的領導人中 。
she said it's helped her to do what she's doing .	她說這是幫助她去做她在做什麼 。
and it was very , very exciting for me to meet her and see just one example of how young people , when they are empowered , given the opportunity to take action , to make the world a better place , truly are our hope for tomorrow .	對我來說 , 非常非常令人興奮 , 看看年輕人的一個例子 , 給予行動的機會 , 讓世界變得更好 , 真的是我們今日的希望 。
artist dianna cohen shares some tough truths about plastic pollution in the ocean and in our lives and some thoughts on how to free ourselves from the plastic gyre .	藝術家dannacohen分享了一些艱難的真理 , 關於海洋中的塑膠污染 , 以及我們生活中的一些思想如何免費塑膠灣 。
consumerism , global issues , green , mission blue , oceans , plastic	消費者、全球議題、綠色、任務藍、海洋、塑膠、塑膠、塑膠 , 、全球性的議題 。
dianna cohen: tough truths about plastic pollution	dannacohen:關於塑膠污染污染的艱難真理 。
i'm a visual artist , and i'm also one of the cofounders of the plastic pollution coalition .	我是一個視覺藝術家 , 我也是塑膠污染的共同創辦人之一 。
i've been working with plastic bags , which i cut up and sew back together as my primary material for my artwork for the last 20 years .	我和塑膠袋一起工作 , 我把我最初的材料分解成我過去20年的藝術品 。
i turn them into two and threedimensional pieces and sculptures and installations .	我把它們變成了兩個三維的碎片和雕塑和裝置 。
upon working with the plastic , after about the first eight years , some of my work started to fissure and break down into smaller little bits of plastic .	在這八年後 , 我有一些工作開始累積 , 分裂成小小的塑膠 。
and i thought , " great .	我心想: 「 太棒了 。
it's ephemeral just like us . "	它就像我們一樣 。 」
upon educating myself a little further about plastics , i actually realized this was a bad thing .	教育自己更進一步的教育塑膠 , 我真的意識到這是一件壞事 。
it's a bad thing that plastic breaks down into smaller little bits , because it's always still plastic .	塑膠會分解成小小的小點 , 因為它總是塑膠 。
and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們所發現的是 , 大部份在海洋環境中 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	在過去幾年 , 我學到了太平洋的垃圾場和gyre 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	我最初的反應 , 我認為這很多人的第一個反應是: 「 天啊 ! 我的天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們必須走出去 , 清理這個東西 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	所以 , 我真的開發了一個建議 , 用一艘自行車 , 和兩組的捕魚垃圾機 , 一台拖車機 , 和一台寒冷的機器 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	我的意圖是 , 要走向gyre , 提高這個議題 , 開始採取塑膠 , 把塑膠裝入一些小小的模塊 , 將它被用來當作建築物 , 以下的社區 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始和那些在海軍環境中一直在研究塑膠問題的人說話 , 我發現 , 把它清理成一個非常小的一滴在世界各地產生了多少 , 實際上我需要回顧更大的照片 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的圖片是:我們需要找到一個方法 , 來阻止它 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要把單一的塑膠分開 , 每天都進入海洋環境 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	所以 , 我也了解到 , 我真的很生氣 。
i wasn't just concerned about plastic that you're trying to imagine out in the middle of the pacific ocean of which i have learned there are now 11 gyres , potentially , of plastic in five major oceans in the world .	我不只關心塑膠你試圖想像在太平洋中間的太平洋中間有11個gre , 可能是世界上五大海裡的塑膠 。
it's not just that gyre of plastic that i'm concerned about it's the gyre of plastic in the supermarket .	不只是我關心的塑膠塑膠 , 是超級市場的塑膠 。
i'd go to the supermarket and all of my food is packaged in plastic .	我會去到超市 , 所有的食物都在塑膠裡包裝 。
all of my beverages are packaged in plastic , even at the health food market .	我所有人都在塑膠裡包裝 , 甚至在健康食物市場 。
i'm also concerned about the plastic in the refrigerator , and i'm concerned about the plastic and the toxins that leach from plastic into us and into our bodies .	我也關心冰箱裡的塑膠 , 我擔心塑膠和塑膠的毒素 , 從塑膠到我們體內 。
so i came together with a group of other people who were all looking at this issue , and we created the plastic pollution coalition .	所以我和一群人一起研究這個議題 , 我們創造了塑膠污染聯盟 。
we have many initiatives that we're working on , but some of them are very basic .	我們有許多我們正在努力的建議 , 但其中的一些是非常基本的 。
one is: if 80 to 90 percent of what we're finding in the ocean of the marine debris that we're finding in the ocean is plastic , then why don't we call it what it is .	一:如果80%到90%的我們在海洋中發現的海洋中發現的海洋是塑膠的 , 那麼為什麼我們不稱它為它是什麼 。
recycling everybody kind of ends their books about being sustainable and greening with the idea of recycling .	回收所有人的書 , 來回收他們的書 , 來回收回收的概念 。
you put something in a bin and you don't have to think about it again .	你把東西放進bin , 你不需要再再思考 。
what is the reality of that ?	什麼是現實呢 ?
in the united states , less than seven percent of our plastics are recycled .	在美國 , 沒有百分之七的塑膠回收 。
and if you really look into it , particularly when it comes to plastic bottles , most of it is only downcycled , or incinerated , or shipped to china .	如果你真的去看它 , 特別是當塑膠瓶時 , 大部分的只是下降 , 或受到緊密 , 或被運送到中國 。
it is downcycled and turned into lesser things , while a glass bottle can be a glass bottle again or can be used again a plastic bottle can never be a plastic bottle again .	它被下降 , 轉化成較少的東西 , 而玻璃瓶可以再次用玻璃瓶 , 或可以再次使用塑膠瓶 , 永遠不會是塑膠瓶 。
so this is a big issue for us .	這對我們來說是個大問題 。
another thing that we're looking at and asking people to think about is we've added a fourth r onto the front of the " reduce , reuse , recycle , " three r's , and that is refuse .	另外一件事 , 我們要問人們思考的是 , 我們加入了四個字母的前方的 「 紅色、回收 」 , 三個r是拒絕的 。
whenever possible , refuse singleuse and disposable plastics .	無論如何 , 拒絕單一的塑膠 。
alternatives exist ; some of them are very oldschool .	替代方案存在 , 有些是很老的學者 。
i myself am now collecting these cool pyrex containers and using those instead of glad and tupperware containers to store food in .	我現在正在收集這些冷酷的x光包器 , 使用這些東西 , 而不是玻璃和豐富的儲存者 , 來儲存食物 。
and i know that i am doing a service to myself and my family .	我知道我是為自己和家人做服務 。
it's very easy to pick up a stainlesssteel bottle or a glass bottle , if you're traveling and you've forgotten to bring your stainlesssteel bottle and fill that up with water or filtered water , versus purchasing plastic bottled water .	很容易拿起一瓶無線電瓶或玻璃瓶 , 如果你在旅行時 , 你就忘了 , 把石油瓶帶到水中或過濾的水裡 , 用塑膠瓶 。
i guess what i want to say to everybody here and i know that you guys know a lot about this issue is that this is a huge problem in the oceans , but this is a problem that we've created as consumers and we can solve .	我猜我想要跟大家說些什麼 , 我知道你們對這個議題知道 , 這問題在於 , 在海洋中 , 這是我們創造的消費者 , 我們可以解決的問題 。
we can solve this by raising awareness of the issue and teaching people to choose alternatives .	我們可以藉由提高議題和教導人們選擇替代方案來解決這個問題 。
so whenever possible , to choose alternatives to singleuse plastics .	所以 , 無論如何 , 選擇替代方案給單一塑膠 。
we can cut the stem tide the stem of this into our oceans and in doing so , save our oceans , save our planet , save ourselves .	我們可以把這首詩縮到我們的海洋中 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的地球 , 拯救我們自己 。
this demo from pattie maes' lab at mit , spearheaded by pranav mistry was the buzz of ted . it's a wearable device with a projector that paves the way for profound interaction with our environment . imagine " minority report " and then some .	由pattiemae實驗室的這個驅動器 , 由pranepre的誤解 , 是ted的buz 。 這是一個可行的裝置 , 用一個專案來維持我們環境的深度互動 。 想像一下: 「 少數的報告 」 , 有些 。
demo , design , interface design , technology	民主、設計、介面設計、科技設計、科技設計、科技設計 。
pattie maes and pranav mistry demo sixthsense	親愛的男孩和豬的錯誤 , 六分之一的敏感度 。
i've been intrigued by this question of whether we could evolve or develop a sixth sense a sense that would give us seamless access and easy access to metainformation or information that may exist somewhere that may be relevant to help us make the right decision about whatever it is that we're coming across .	我對這個問題感到很感興趣 , 是否能演化或開發出六個感知 , 一種感知 , 讓我們無法取得密碼和簡單的資訊 , 可能存在於某些地方 , 幫助我們做出正確的決策 , 不論我們要跨越什麼 。
and some of you may argue , well , don't today's cell phones do that already ?	有些人可能會說 , 嗯 , 今天的手機已經沒用了嗎 ?
but i would say no .	但我會說不 。
when you meet someone here at ted and this is the top networking place , of course , of the year you don't shake somebody's hand and then say , " can you hold on for a moment while i take out my phone and google you ? "	當你在ted見面時 , 這裡是最頂尖的網絡 , 當然 , 你不喜歡某人的手 , 然後說: 「 你能不能在我拿出手機 , google你嗎 ? 」
or when you go to the supermarket and you're standing there in that huge aisle of different types of toilet papers , you don't take out your cell phone , and open a browser , and go to a website to try to decide which of these different toilet papers is the most ecologically responsible purchase to make .	或者 , 當你去超市時 , 你站在那裡 , 站在一個大型不同的廁所中 , 你不會拿你的手機 , 打開瀏覽器 , 去嘗試決定這些不同的廁所是最可負責的購物 。
so we don't really have easy access to all this relevant information that can just help us make optimal decisions about what to do next and what actions to take .	所以 , 我們沒有很容易取得這些相關的資訊 , 才能協助我們做出最佳的決定 , 來做下一步和行動 。
and so my research group at the media lab has been developing a series of inventions to give us access to this information in a sort of easy way , without requiring that the user changes any of their behavior .	所以 , 我在媒體實驗室的研究團隊已經開發了一系列的發明 , 以一種簡單的方式提供這些資訊 , 不用使用者改變他們的行為 。
and i'm here to unveil our latest effort , and most successful effort so far , which is still very much a work in process .	我來這裡要揭露我們最新的努力 , 最成功的努力 , 目前 , 目前還在過程中 , 這項工作很大 。
i'm actually wearing the device right now and we've sort of cobbled it together with components that are off the shelf and that , by the way , only cost 350 dollars at this point in time .	我現在正穿著這個裝置 , 然後我們將它結合在一起 , 把它們結合在一起 , 順便說一下 , 時間只有350美金 。
i'm wearing a camera , just a simple webcam , a portable , batterypowered projection system with a little mirror .	我穿著攝影機 , 只是一個簡單的網誌 , 可攜帶、電池的專案系統 , 和一個小鏡子 。
these components communicate to my cell phone in my pocket which acts as the communication and computation device .	這些元件跟我的手機溝通 , 在我的口袋裡 , 作為溝通和計算設備 。
and in the video here we see my student pranav mistry , who's really the genius who's been implementing and designing this whole system .	在這段影片中 , 我們看到我的學生的意見 , 他們真的是天才 , 他們正在執行和設計整個系統 。
and we see how this system lets him walk up to any surface and start using his hands to interact with the information that is projected in front of him .	我們看到這個系統如何讓他走上任何表面 , 開始用他的手來和他面前的資訊互動 。
the system tracks the four significant fingers .	系統追蹤了四個巨大的手指 。
in this case , he's wearing simple marker caps that you may recognize .	在這個案例中 , 他穿著簡單的標記帽子 , 你可能知道 。
but if you want a more stylish version you could also paint your nails in different colors .	但如果你想要更加精緻的版本 , 你也可以在不同的顏色上畫你的細節 。
and the camera basically tracks these four fingers and recognizes any gestures that he's making so he can just go to , for example , a map of long beach , zoom in and out , etc .	相機基本上追蹤了這四個手指 , 辨識出他所製造的任何特徵 , 例如 , 一個長灘的地圖 , 放大 , 等等 。
the system also recognizes iconic gestures such as the " take a picture " gesture , and then takes a picture of whatever is in front of you .	系統也能辨識出像 「 拍一張照片 」 的形象 , 然後拍一張你面前的照片 。
and when he then walks back to the media lab , he can just go up to any wall and project all the pictures that he's taken , sort through them and organize them , and resize them , etc . , again using all natural gestures .	當他走回媒體實驗室時 , 他就可以去任何牆壁 , 專案他所拍攝的照片 , 包括它們 , 組織它們 , 等等 , 再次使用所有自然的姿勢 。
so , some of you most likely were here two years ago and saw the demo by jeff han or some of you may think , " well , doesn't this look like the microsoft surface table ? "	所以 , 有些人可能在兩年前就在這裡 , 看到傑夫•漢 , 有些人可能會想: 「 嗯 , 這看起來不像微軟的表面桌子 ? 」
and yes , you also interact using natural gestures , both hands , etc .	沒錯 , 你也用天然的姿勢互動 , 雙手等等 。
but the difference here is that you can use any surface , you can walk to up to any surface , including your hand if nothing else is available and interact with this projected data .	但差別是 , 你可以用任何表面 , 你可以走到任何表面 , 包括你的手 , 如果沒有任何東西可以使用 , 和這個專案資料互動 。
the device is completely portable , and can be . . .	裝置是完全可攜帶的 , 可是......
so one important difference is that it's totally mobile .	一個很重要的差異是 , 它是完全移動的 。
another even more important difference is that in mass production this would not cost more tomorrow than today's cell phones and would actually not sort of be a bigger packaging could look a lot more stylish than this version that i'm wearing around my neck .	另一個更重要的差異是 , 在大眾生產 , 這不會比現今的手機更明顯 , 實際上 , 不像一個更大的包裝 , 看起來比我穿著脖子的版本還要多 。
but other than letting some of you live out your fantasy of looking as cool as tom cruise in " minority report , " the reason why we're really excited about this device is that it really can act as one of these sixthsense devices that gives you relevant information about whatever is in front of you .	但 , 除了讓有些人活在你的幻想中 , 看起來很酷 , 像是 「 少數報告報告 」 , 原因是我們對於這個裝置感到興奮的原因是 , 它真的可以扮演出在你面前的第六個裝置 。
so we see pranav here going into the supermarket and he's shopping for some paper towels .	所以 , 我們在這裡看到的是 「 超市 」 , 他在購買一些紙巾 。
and , as he picks up a product the system can recognize the product that he's picking up , using either image recognition or marker technology , and give him the green light or an orange light .	當他拿起一個產品 , 系統就能辨識出他拿起的產品 , 使用圖像辨識或標記技術 , 給他綠光或橘光 。
he can ask for additional information .	他可以要求更多的資訊 。
so this particular choice here is a particularly good choice , given his personal criteria .	所以這個特定的選擇是特別好的選擇 , 給予他個人的批判 。
some of you may want the toilet paper with the most bleach in it rather than the most ecologicallyresponsible choice .	有些人可能想把廁所的紙和最大麻煩 , 而不是最有責任的生態選擇 。
if he picks up a book in the bookstore , he can get an amazon rating it gets projected right on the cover of the book .	如果他在書中挑一本書 , 他可以拿到亞馬遜的比賽 , 它就在書的封面上投射 。
this is juan's book , our previous speaker , which gets a great rating , by the way , at amazon .	這是jan的書 , 我們先前的演講者 , 順便說一下 , 亞馬遜的評價很大 。
and so , pranav turns the page of the book and can then see additional information about the book reader comments , maybe sort of information by his favorite critic , etc .	所以 , 帕爾維將這本書的頁面 , 看看書讀者的內容 , 也許是他最喜歡的批評 , 等等 。
if he turns to a particular page he finds an annotation by maybe an expert of a friend of ours that gives him a little bit of additional information about whatever is on that particular page .	如果他轉向一個特定的頁面 , 他會找到一個信念 , 也許是一位朋友的專家 , 給他一點額外的資訊 , 關於任何特定的頁面 。
reading the newspaper it never has to be outdated .	閱讀報紙 , 永遠不會被外出 。
you can get video annotations of the event that you're reading about you can get the latest sports scores etc .	你可以得到你在閱讀的事件的影片 , 你可以得到最新的運動比例等等 。
this is a more controversial one .	這是更具爭議性的一件事 。
as you interact with someone at ted , maybe you can see a word cloud of the tags , the words that are associated with that person in their blog and personal web pages .	當你和ted的某人互動時 , 或許你能看到一個 「 標籤 」 這個詞 , 和那個人的部落格和個人網頁有關 。
in this case , the student is interested in cameras , etc .	在這個例子中 , 學生對攝影機有興趣 。
on your way to the airport , if you pick up your boarding pass , it can tell you that your flight is delayed , that the gate has changed , etc .	在你走到機場上 , 如果你拿起你的板子 , 它可以告訴你你的飛行已經被破壞了 , 蓋茲已經改變了 , 等等 。
and , if you need to know what the current time is it's as simple as drawing a watch on your arm .	若你需要知道目前的當下時間是什麼 , 它就好像在你的手臂上繪畫一個眼睛 。
so that's where we're at so far in developing this sixth sense that would give us seamless access to all this relevant information about the things that we may come across .	所以 , 目前我們在開發這個第六個感知 , 讓我們無法取得這些相關的資訊 , 關於我們能跨越的事物 。
my student pranav , who's really , like i said , the genius behind this .	我的學生們 , 其實 , 我說的 , 像我說的 , 這背後的天才 。
he does deserve a lot of applause because i don't think he's slept much in the last three months , actually .	他的確值得很高興 , 因為我不認為他在過去三個月內睡得太多 , 事實上 。
and his girlfriend is probably not very happy about him either .	他的女友可能對他來說不高興 。
but it's not perfect yet , it's very much a work in progress .	但這還不是完美的 , 在進步過程中 , 是非常多的 。
and who knows , maybe in another 10 years we'll be here with the ultimate sixth sense brain implant .	誰知道 , 也許在接下來的十年裡 , 我們將來會和第六感官的腦植入在一起 。
phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	2001年9月11日 , 艾瑞克•羅斯和阿加爾有強大的友誼 , 羅德里茲的兒子被殺害了 , 2001年9月11日 , elwafi的兒子zarussauui被禁止在那些攻擊中被禁止 , 提供了一名生命的句子 。
culture , global issues , politics	文化、全球政治、政治、政治 。
9/11 healing: the mothers who found forgiveness , friendship	9/11的治癒:被發現寬恕、友誼的母親 。
phyllis rodriguez: we are here today because of the fact that we have what most people consider an unusual friendship .	博士•羅德里茲:今天我們在這裡 , 是因為我們有最多人認為一個不尋常的友誼 。
and yet , it feels natural to us now .	然而 , 對我們來說 , 感覺很自然 。
i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我首先發現 , 我的兒子在191年9月11日到2001年9月11日 。
we didn't know if he had perished yet until 36 hours later .	我們還不知道他是否有活下來 , 直到36小時後 。
at the time , we knew that it was political .	當時 , 我們知道它是政治的 。
we were afraid of what our country was going to do in the name of our son my husband , orlando , and i and our family .	我們害怕我們的國家會怎麼做 , 在我們兒子的名字中 , 我的丈夫 , 奧地蘭多 , 我和我們的家人 。
and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到它時 , 經過震驚 , 恐怖的震驚 , 我們的生活中最糟糕的爆炸 , 其實 , 我們並沒有被強化 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾週後 , zacarariasmosaui已經指出六個對抗恐怖主義的懲罰 , 美國政府稱他為死刑 , 假如我和我的丈夫和公開討論 。
through that and through human rights groups , we were brought together with several other victims' families .	透過這個 , 透過人權團體 , 我們帶了許多其他受害者的家庭 。
when i saw aicha in the media , coming over when her son was indicted , and i thought , " what a brave woman .	當我在媒體上看到阿拉伯 , 當她兒子被警告時 , 我心想: 「 勇敢的女人 。
someday i want to meet that woman when i'm stronger . "	有一天 , 我想要和那個女人見面 。 」
i was still in deep grief ; i knew i didn't have the strength .	我還在深深的悲慟中 , 我知道我沒有力量 。
i knew i would find her someday , or we would find each other .	我知道我有一天會找到她 , 或者我們會互相找到彼此 。
because , when people heard that my son was a victim , i got immediate sympathy .	因為 , 當人們聽到我的兒子是受害者 , 我馬上就有同情 。
but when people learned what her son was accused of , she didn't get that sympathy .	但當人們知道她兒子被指控的時候 , 她沒有同情心 。
but her suffering is equal to mine .	但她的苦難和我一樣 。
so we met in november 2002 , and aicha will now tell you how that came about .	所以 , 我們在2002年11月見面 , 阿加哈現在會告訴你這怎麼來 。
aicha elwafi: good afternoon , ladies and gentlemen .	aichaelwafi:好的下午 , 女士和先生們 。
i am the mother of zacarias moussaoui .	我是zacarariamoussaui的母親 。
and i asked the organization of human rights to put me in touch with the parents of the victims .	我問了人類權利的組織 , 讓我和受害者的父母接觸 。
so they introduced me to five families .	所以他們把我介紹給五個家庭 。
and i saw phyllis , and i watched her .	我看到了phyllis , 我看著她 。
she was the only mother in the group .	她是團體中唯一的母親 。
the others were brothers , sisters .	其他人是兄弟姐妹 。
and i saw in her eyes that she was a mother , just like me .	我看到她的眼睛 , 她是個母親 , 就像我一樣 。
i suffered a lot as a mother .	身為一個母親 , 我受苦很多 。
i was married when i was 14 .	我14歲時結婚 。
i lost a child when i was 15 , a second child when i was 16 .	當我十五歲時 , 我在十六歲時失去了一個孩子 。
so the story with zacarias was too much really .	所以 , zacaria的故事太多了 。
and i still suffer , because my son is like he's buried alive .	我仍然受苦 , 因為我的兒子就像他活著一樣 。
i know she really cried for her son .	我知道她真的哭了她兒子 。
but she knows where he is .	但她知道他在哪裡 。
my son , i don't know where he is .	我的兒子 , 我不知道他在哪裡 。
i don't know if he's alive . i don't know if he's tortured .	我不知道他是否活著 , 我不知道他是否有害 。
i don't know what happened to him .	我不知道他發生了什麼事 。
so that's why i decided to tell my story , so that my suffering is something positive for other women .	因此 , 這就是為什麼我決定說我的故事 , 所以我的苦難對其他女性來說是正面的 。
for all the women , all the mothers that give life , you can give back , you can change .	對所有婦女 , 所有給予生命的母親 , 你可以回饋 , 你可以改變 。
it's up to us women , because we are women , because we love our children .	我們是女性 , 因為我們是女性 , 因為我們喜歡我們的孩子 。
we must be handinhand and do something together .	我們必須是手手 , 一起做點什麼 。
it's not against women , it's for us , for us women , for our children .	這不是對女性來說 , 對我們來說 , 對女性來說 , 對我們的孩子來說 , 對我們的孩子 。
i talk against violence , against terrorism .	我對抗暴力 , 反對恐怖主義 。
i go to schools to talk to young , muslim girls so they don't accept to be married against their will very young .	我去學校和年輕的穆斯林女孩談話 , 讓他們不接受結婚 , 反對他們的意志很年輕 。
so if i can save one of the young girls , and avoid that they get married and suffer as much as i did , well this is something good .	所以如果我能拯救其中一位年輕女孩 , 避免他們結婚和苦難 , 如我所做的 , 這是一件好事 。
this is why i'm here in front of you .	這就是我在你們面前的原因 。
pr: i would like to say that i have learned so much from aicha , starting with that day we had our very first meeting with other family members which was a very private meeting with security , because it was november 2002 , and , frankly , we were afraid of the superpatriotism of that time in the country those of us family members .	帕特:我想說 , 我從阿加哈學到這麼多 , 從那天開始 , 我們和其他家庭成員一起參加一個非常私人的會議 , 因為那是2002年11月 , 坦白說 , 我們害怕那個時代的超級抗議主義主義者 。
but we were all so nervous .	但我們都很緊張 。
" why does she want to meet us ? "	「 為什麼她要跟我們見面 ? 」
and then she was nervous .	然後她很緊張 。
" why did we want to meet her ? "	「 我們為什麼要見她 ? 」
what did we want from each other ?	我們對彼此想要什麼呢 ?
before we knew each others' names , or anything , we had embraced and wept .	在我們認識彼此的名字之前 , 或任何東西 , 我們都在擁抱和無線網路上 。
then we sat in a circle with support , with help , from people experienced in this kind of reconciliation .	接著 , 我們坐在一個與支持的圈子中 , 從人體驗到這種相互聯繫 。
and aicha started , and she said , " i don't know if my son is guilty or innocent , but i want to tell you how sorry i am for what happened to your families .	艾卡開始 , 她說: 「 我不知道我的兒子是否是罪惡或無辜 , 但我想告訴你們 , 我對你的家人有多抱歉 。
i know what it is to suffer , and i feel that if there is a crime , a person should be tried fairly and punished . "	我知道這是什麼是痛苦的 , 我覺得如果有犯罪 , 一個人應該很公平地嘗試和懲罰 。 」
but she reached out to us in that way , and it was , i'd like to say , it was an icebreaker .	但她在那方面向我們伸出去 , 我想說 , 這是個冰箱 。
and what happened then is we all told our stories , and we all connected as human beings .	接下來發生的是 , 我們都告訴我們的故事 , 我們都與人類連結在一起 。
by the end of the afternoon it was about three hours after lunch we'd felt as if we'd known each other forever .	在午餐後結束時 , 大約有三小時 , 我們就會感覺到 , 就像我們永遠都知道的一樣 。
now what i learned from her , is a woman , not only who could be so generous under these present circumstances and what it was then , and what was being done to her son , but the life she's had .	我從她身上學到的 , 是一位女人 , 不只能在現場的環境下被遺傳的情況下 , 以及當時的狀況 , 以及她的兒子做了什麼 , 但她有的生命 。
i never had met someone with such a hard life , from such a totally different culture and environment from my own .	我從來沒有遇過這種艱難生活的人 , 從這個完全不同的文化和環境來源 。
and i feel that we have a special connection , which i value very much .	我覺得我們有特殊的連結 , 我非常重視 。

okay , now for the science bit .	好的 , 現在 , 為科學方面 。
before lifesaver , the best hand filters were only capable of filtering down to about 200 nanometers .	在生命總署之前 , 最好的濾器只能過濾到大約200奈米 。
the smallest bacteria is about 200 nanometers .	最小的細菌大約是200奈米 。
so a 200nanometer bacteria is going to get through a 200nanometer hole .	所以 , 一個200奈米的細菌將會經過200奈米的洞 。
the smallest virus , on the other hand , is about 25 nanometers .	另一方面 , 最小的病毒大約是25奈米 。
so that's definitely going to get through those 200 nanometer holes .	所以這絕對是要穿越那200奈米的洞 。
lifesaver pores are 15 nanometers .	生命的面積是15奈米 。
so nothing is getting through .	所以 , 什麼都沒有發生 。

traditionally , in a crisis , what do we do ?	傳統來說 , 在危機中 , 我們該怎麼做 ?

diseases spread . more resources are required .	疾病散播 , 更多資源都需要 。

using the old thinking , of national infrastructure and pipe work , is too expensive .	用舊的思考 , 國家基礎建設和pipe工作 , 太昂貴了 。
when you run the numbers on a calculator , you run out of noughts .	當你在計算機運行時 , 你就跑出笑聲 。

instead of shipping water , and using manmade processes to do it , let's use mother nature . she's got a fantastic system .	不用運輸水 , 用人造程序來做 , 讓我們用大自然 。 她有很棒的系統 。
she picks the water up from there , desalinates it , for free , transports it over there , and dumps it onto the mountains , rivers , and streams .	她從那裡拿出水 , 把水放進去 , 把它放到那邊 , 把它放到山上 , 河流和溪流中 。

this will process 25 , 000 liters of water ; that's good enough for a family of four , for three years .	這會處理25000公尺的水 , 這對四個家庭來說是夠好的 , 三年來 。

about half a cent a day to run .	大約有一天半分之一的跑步 。
so , by thinking differently , and processing water at the point of use , mothers and children no longer have to walk four hours a day to collect their water .	所以 , 用不同的方式思考 , 在使用時期 , 母親和孩子們不再需要每天四個小時才能收集他們的水 。
they can get it from a source nearby .	它們可以從附近的來源取得它 。
so with just eight billion dollars , we can hit the millennium goal's target of halving the number of people without access to safe drinking water .	所以 , 只有八十億美金 , 我們可以打擊千禧年的目標 , 讓人們無法取得安全飲用水 。
to put that into context , the u . k . government spends about 12 billion pounds a year on foreign aid .	為了將這點放到情境上 , 美國政府每年花了大約12億磅的外國援助 。
but why stop there ?	但為什麼要停下來呢 ?
with 20 billion dollars , everyone can have access to safe drinking water .	有20億美元 , 每個人都能取得安全飲用水 。
so the threeandahalf billion people that suffer every year as a result , and the two million kids that die every year , will live .	所以 , 每年有三十億人每年受苦 , 每年有兩百萬個孩子死亡 , 將會活下來 。
paddy ashdown claims that we are living in a moment in history where power is changing in ways it never has before . in a spellbinding talk at tedxbrussels he outlines the three major global shifts that he sees coming .	廣播廣告宣稱我們在歷史上 , 在歷史上 , 權力正在改變它以前從來沒有過的方式 。 在tedxussel的演講中 , 他指出他所看到的三大轉變 。
foreign policy , global issues , politics , world cultures	外國政策、全球議題、政治、世界文化文化、世界文化 。
paddy ashdown: the global power shift	adadden:全球的權力轉變 , 轉變了 。
there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在19世紀末 , 有一首詩被一首非常著名的英文詩人寫作 。
it was said to echo in churchill's brain in the 1930s .	在1930年代 , 伊斯蘭的大腦被告知 。
and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die . "	首詩說: 「 夏天 , 夏天 , 躺在溪流中 , 我聽到一個遙遠的戲劇家 , 鼓動了 , 像一個在夢中、遙遠、附近、低潮的路上 , 被朋友和食物傳送 , 很快就死了 。 」
those who are interested in poetry , the poem is " a shropshire lad " written by a . e . housman .	那些對詩有興趣的人 , 詩是 「 一名商店女士 」 寫的 , 由一名荷蘭人寫的 。
but what housman understood , and you hear it in the symphonies of nielsen too , was that the long , hot , silvan summers of stability of the 19th century were coming to a close , and that we were about to move into one of those terrifying periods of history when power changes .	但 , 霍斯曼明白了什麼 , 你也聽到在尼爾斯的理論中 , 是19世紀的長期、熱熱和的夏天 , 我們將要搬到其中一個恐怖的歷史改變時期 。
and these are always periods , ladies and gentlemen , accompanied by turbulence , and all too often by blood .	這些都是經常的時期 , 女士們先生們 , 被摧殘的 , 常常常被血流傳染 。
and my message for you is that i believe we are condemned , if you like , to live at just one of those moments in history when the gimbals upon which the established order of power is beginning to change and the new look of the world , the new powers that exist in the world , are beginning to take form .	而我的訊息是 , 我相信我們已經被認定了 , 如果你想要活在歷史上 , 其中一個時刻 , 當最新的力量開始改變和世界的新角度 , 正開始採取形式 。
and these are and we see it very clearly today nearly always highly turbulent times , highly difficult times , and all too often very bloody times .	現今 , 我們很明顯地看到它 , 幾乎總是高度不穩定的時機 , 很困難 , 很多時候都很血 。
by the way , it happens about once every century .	順便一提 , 每一世紀發生了 。
you might argue that the last time it happened and that's what housman felt coming and what churchill felt too was that when power passed from the old nations , the old powers of europe , across the atlantic to the new emerging power of the united states of america the beginning of the american century .	你可能會說 , 上次發生了 , 這是霍華曼的感覺 , 以及教會的感覺 , 當權力來自舊國家 , 歐洲的舊權力 , 橫跨美國的大西洋 , 美國的新興力量 。
and of course , into the vacuum where the tooold european powers used to be were played the two bloody catastrophes of the last century the one in the first part and the one in the second part: the two great world wars .	當然 , 在真空中 , 當時的歐洲權力被用來扮演上個世紀的二個血液災難 , 第二個部分:兩個偉大的世界戰爭 。
mao zedong used to refer to them as the european civil wars , and it's probably a more accurate way of describing them .	麥隆曾經把他們稱為歐洲大戰 , 可能是更精確的描述方式來描述它們 。
well , ladies and gentlemen , we live at one of those times .	各位先生女士 , 我們住在其中一個時代 。
but for us , i want to talk about three factors today .	但對我們來說 , 我今天要談談三個因素 。
and the first of these , the first two of these , is about a shift in power .	首先 , 首先 , 這兩個 , 重點在於權力的轉變 。
and the second is about some new dimension which i want to refer to , which has never quite happened in the way it's happening now .	第二個是關於我想要重建的新維度 , 這從來沒有發生在它現在發生的情況下 。
but let's talk about the shifts of power that are occurring to the world .	但 , 讓我們來談談世界上的權力轉變 。
and what is happening today is , in one sense , frightening because it's never happened before .	今天正在發生的事是 , 一方面來說 , 很害怕 , 因為它從來沒有發生過 。
we have seen lateral shifts of power the power of greece passed to rome and the power shifts that occurred during the european civilizations but we are seeing something slightly different .	我們看過後的力量轉變了希臘的力量 , 在歐洲文明中發生的力量 , 我們看到了一些不一樣的東西 。
for power is not just moving laterally from nation to nation .	權力不僅僅是從國家到國家 。
it's also moving vertically .	它也在垂直移動 。
what's happening today is that the power that was encased , held to accountability , held to the rule of law , within the institution of the nation state has now migrated in very large measure onto the global stage .	今天的情況是 , 被監禁的權力 , 對於法律的規則 , 以法律的制度來移植在全球階段的大量測量 。
the globalization of power we talk about the globalization of markets , but actually it's the globalization of real power .	全球化的權力 , 我們談到市場的全球化 , 但實際上是真正的權力 。
and where , at the nation state level that power is held to accountability subject to the rule of law , on the international stage it is not .	在這個國家國家的層級 , 權力是對法律規則的負責主題 , 在國際舞台上 , 並非如此 。
the international stage and the global stage where power now resides: the power of the internet , the power of the satellite broadcasters , the power of the money changers this vast moneygoround that circulates now 32 times the amount of money necessary for the trade it's supposed to be there to finance the money changers , if you like , the financial speculators that have brought us all to our knees quite recently , the power of the multinational corporations now developing budgets often bigger than mediumsized countries .	國際階段和全球階段 , 現在的權力是:網路的力量 , 衛星廣播廣播者的力量 , 這項大量的金錢改革 , 如今交易的必要費用的費用 , 應該要有金錢改善金錢的改革 , 如果你喜歡 , 財務的推動者 , 最近我們所有人都帶給我們的膝蓋爾的公司 。
these live in a global space which is largely unregulated , not subject to the rule of law , and in which people may act free of constraint .	這些生活在一個巨大的全球空間中 , 不是被監控的法律規則 , 人們可能選擇自由的限制 。
now that suits the powerful up to a moment .	現在 , 這套裝置是很強大的 。
it's always suitable for those who have the most power to operate in spaces without constraint , but the lesson of history is that , sooner or later , unregulated space space not subject to the rule of law becomes populated , not just by the things you wanted international trade , the internet , etc . but also by the things you don't want international criminality , international terrorism .	對那些沒有限制的空間的人來說 , 總是能有最多的權力 , 但歷史的教訓是 , 不久後 , 不管法律的規則 , 不只因為你想要國際貿易、網路 , 等等 , 你不想說國際犯罪、國際恐怖主義 。
the revelation of 9/11 is that even if you are the most powerful nation on earth , nevertheless , those who inhabit that space can attack you even in your most iconic of cities one bright september morning .	911事件的揭示 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 不然 , 那些居住空間的人甚至可以在你最明顯的城市早上攻擊你 。
it's said that something like 60 percent of the four million dollars that was taken to fund 9/11 actually passed through the institutions of the twin towers which 9/11 destroyed .	它說 , 大約有百分之六十五十萬美金 , 由911的資金來資助911大樓的機構 , 可是9/11摧毀了 。
you see , our enemies also use this space the space of mass travel , the internet , satellite broadcasters to be able to get around their poison , which is about destroying our systems and our ways .	你看 , 我們的敵人也使用這個空間 , 大規模旅行、網路、衛星廣播者 , 來在他們的毒品中取得 , 就是破壞我們的系統和路 。
sooner or later , sooner or later , the rule of history is that where power goes governance must follow .	不久後 , 不久後 , 歷史的規則是 , 權力在哪裡要遵循 。
and if it is therefore the case , as i believe it is , that one of the phenomenon of our time is the globalization of power , then it follows that one of the challenges of our time is to bring governance to the global space .	假如我相信這個案例是 , 我們當時的一個現象是全球化的力量 , 那麼 , 我們的時間挑戰的其中一個挑戰就是將國際空間帶進去 。
and i believe that the decades ahead of us now will be to a greater or lesser extent turbulent the more or less we are able to achieve that aim: to bring governance to the global space .	我相信 , 數十年來 , 我們現在會變得更大或更少 , 我們能達成目標:將國際空間帶進國際空間 。
now notice , i'm not talking about government .	注意一下 , 我不是在談政府 。
i'm not talking about setting up some global democratic institution .	我不是在說要建立一些全球民主機構 。
my own view , by the way , ladies and gentlemen , is that this is unlikely to be done by spawning more u . n . institutions .	順帶一提 , 我自己的觀點 , 各位先生女士們 , 這不太可能是用更多的聯合國機構來做 。
if we didn't have the u . n . , we'd have to invent it .	如果我們沒有聯合國 , 我們就得要發明它 。
the world needs an international forum .	世界需要國際論壇 。
it needs a means by which you can legitimize international action .	它需要一個意義 , 你可以合法化國際行動 。
but when it comes to governance of the global space , my guess is this won't happen through the creation of more u . n . institutions .	但當它來到全球空間的治理時 , 我的猜測是 , 這不會發生越多聯合國機構 。
it will actually happen by the powerful coming together and making treatybased systems , treatybased agreements , to govern that global space .	實際上 , 強大的成果會發生 , 以治療為基礎的系統、治療協議 , 來管理這個全球空間 。
and if you look , you can see them happening , already beginning to emerge .	如果你看 , 你可以看到它們正在發生 , 已經開始出現了 。
the world trade organization: treatybased organization , entirely treatybased , and yet , powerful enough to hold even the most powerful , the united states , to account if necessary .	世界貿易組織:治療基礎組織 , 完全依賴基礎 , 然而 , 強大的確保美國最強大、美國 , 如果必要的話 。
kyoto: the beginnings of struggling to create a treatybased organization .	kyoto:努力創造一個治療基礎組織的開端 。
the g20: we know now that we have to put together an institution which is capable of bringing governance to that financial space for financial speculation .	g20:我們現在知道 , 我們必須組成一個機構 , 讓金融空間可以把政府改善為財務空間 。
and that's what the g20 is , a treatybased institution .	這就是g20的樣子 , 一個以治療為基礎的機構 。
now there's a problem there , and we'll come back to it in a minute , which is that if you bring the most powerful together to make the rules in treatybased institutions , to fill that governance space , then what happens to the weak who are left out ?	這裡有一個問題 , 我們會再回來 , 一分鐘後 , 若你把最強大的結合在一起 , 把規則放在治療的制度上 , 去填補那些治理空間 , 那麼那些離開的弱點呢 ?
and that's a big problem , and we'll return to it in just a second .	這是個大問題 , 我們會再回到一秒鐘 。
so there's my first message , that if you are to pass through these turbulent times more or less turbulently , then our success in doing that will in large measure depend on our capacity to bring sensible governance to the global space .	所以 , 我的第一個訊息是 , 如果你要通過這些不穩定的時機 , 那麼我們的成功會在大規模的測量程度下依賴我們對全球空間帶來敏感的治理 。
and watch that beginning to happen .	看看這開始發生 。
my second point is , and i know i don't have to talk to an audience like this about such a thing , but power is not just shifting vertically , it's also shifting horizontally .	我的第二點是 , 我知道我不需要和像這樣的觀眾談話 , 但權力不僅僅是垂直轉變 , 也改變了地平線 。
you might argue that the story , the history of civilizations , has been civilizations gathered around seas with the first ones around the mediterranean , the more recent ones in the ascendents of western power around the atlantic .	你可能會說 , 文明的歷史 , 文明的歷史 , 被文明聚集在海平面上 , 最近期的西方權力在大西洋 。
well it seems to me that we're now seeing a fundamental shift of power , broadly speaking , away from nations gathered around the atlantic [seaboard] to the nations gathered around the pacific rim .	對我來說 , 我們現在看到一個基本的權力轉變 , 廣泛地說話 , 從大西洋的國家聚集到太平洋的河流 。
now that begins with economic power , but that's the way it always begins .	這從經濟力量開始 , 但那就是它總是開始的 。
you already begin to see the development of foreign policies , the augmentation of military budgets occurring in the other growing powers in the world .	你已經開始看到外交政策的發展 , 軍事預算的擴增 , 在世界上其他的增長權力 。
i think actually this is not so much a shift from the west to the east ; something different is happening .	我認為這不是從西方轉移到東方 ; 有些不同的事情正在發生 。
my guess is , for what it's worth , is that the united states will remain the most powerful nation on earth for the next 10 years , 15 , but the context in which she holds her power has now radically altered ; it has radically changed .	我的猜測是 , 值得注意的是 , 美國會維持未來十年最強大的國家 , 十五年來 , 但她的權力已經徹底改變了 ; 它已經徹底改變了 。
we are coming out of 50 years , most unusual years , of history in which we have had a totally monopolar world , in which every compass needle for or against has to be referenced by its position to washington a world bestrode by a single colossus .	我們從50年來 , 最不尋常的年來 , 我們有著完全獨立世界的歷史 , 每一針都要對華盛頓的位置來接觸一個單獨的同步世界 。
but that's not a usual case in history .	但這不是歷史上常見的案例 。
in fact , what's now emerging is the much more normal case of history .	事實上 , 現在的新興是歷史上最正常的案例 。
you're beginning to see the emergence of a multipolar world .	你開始看到一個多個世界的出現 。
up until now , the united states has been the dominant feature of our world .	直到現在 , 美國一直是我們世界的主要特徵 。
they will remain the most powerful nation , but they will be the most powerful nation in an increasingly multipolar world .	他們會維持最強大的國家 , 但他們會成為更強大的國家 , 在越來越多世界中 。
and you begin to see the alternative centers of power building up in china , of course , though my own guess is that china's ascent to greatness is not smooth .	當然 , 你開始看到中國的電力建設的替代中心 , 雖然我自己的猜測是中國的優秀是不滑的 。
it's going to be quite grumpy as china begins to democratize her society after liberalizing her economy .	隨著中國開始將她的社會民主化 , 在自由化經濟之後 , 將會變得很痛苦 。
but that's a subject of a different discussion .	但這是一個不同的討論的主題 。
you see india , you see brazil .	你看到印度 , 你看到巴西 。
you see increasingly that the world now looks actually , for us europeans , much more like europe in the 19th century .	你愈來愈來愈來愈來愈來愈來愈像19世紀的歐洲人
europe in the 19th century: a great british foreign secretary , lord canning , used to describe it as the " european concert of powers . "	在19世紀 , 歐洲:一個偉大的英國外國秘密 , 雷德•加爾 , 曾經描述它是《歐洲的權力協會》 。
there was a balance , a fivesided balance .	有一個平衡 , 一個五個平衡 。
britain always played to the balance .	英國經常扮演平衡 。
if paris got together with berlin , britain got together with vienna and rome to provide a counterbalance .	如果巴黎和柏林合作 , 英國和維納和羅馬一起合作 , 來提供對抗性 。
now notice , in a period which is dominated by a monopolar world , you have fixed alliances nato , the warsaw pact .	注意到 , 在一個月經中 , 由一個獨立世界主導 , 你已經修正了娜拉多 , 戰場的平台 。
a fixed polarity of power means fixed alliances .	一個固定的權力 , 意味著固定聯盟 。
but a multiple polarity of power means shifting and changing alliances .	但有多的力量 , 意味著轉變和改變聯盟 。
and that's the world we're coming into , in which we will increasingly see that our alliances are not fixed .	這就是我們來到的世界 , 我們將會越來越明白我們的盟友不是固定的 。
canning , the great british foreign secretary once said , " britain has a common interest , but no common allies . "	加拿大 , 英國外國秘密曾經說過: 「 英國有共同的利益 , 但沒有共同的盟友 。 」
and we will see increasingly that even we in the west will reach out , have to reach out , beyond the cozy circle of the atlantic powers to make alliances with others if we want to get things done in the world .	我們會越來越看到 , 即使我們在西方 , 要達成 , 遠遠超過大西洋的大西洋電路 , 和其他人合作 , 如果我們想在世界各地做事 。
note , that when we went into libya , it was not good enough for the west to do it alone ; we had to bring others in .	記住 , 當我們進入利比亞時 , 西方不夠好 , 不夠好 。 我們必須把其他人帶進來 。
we had to bring , in this case , the arab league in .	我們必須把阿拉伯聯盟帶進來 。
my guess is iraq and afghanistan are the last times when the west has tried to do it themselves , and we haven't succeeded .	我的猜測是伊拉克和阿富汗 , 當西方試圖自己做 , 我們就沒成功了 。
my guess is that we're reaching the beginning of the end of 400 years i say 400 years because it's the end of the ottoman empire of the hegemony of western power , western institutions and western values .	我的猜測是 , 我們在400年末的開端 , 我說了400年 , 因為它是西方權力的最末端 , 西方機構和西方價值觀 。
you know , up until now , if the west got its act together , it could propose and dispose in every corner of the world .	你知道 , 直到現在 , 如果西方的行動 , 它可以在世界各角落中提取和分離 。
but that's no longer true .	但這不再是真實的 。
take the last financial crisis after the second world war .	以第二次世界大戰後 , 最後的財務危機 。
the west got together the bretton woods institution , world bank , international monetary fund the problem solved .	西方集合了布雷頓森林機構 , 世界銀行、國際網路網路基金解決了問題 。
now we have to call in others .	現在我們必須打電話給其他人 。
now we have to create the g20 .	現在我們必須創造g20 。
now we have to reach beyond the cozy circle of our western friends .	現在我們必須超越西方朋友的同理心圈 。
let me make a prediction for you , which is probably even more startling .	讓我為你做出一個預測 , 這可能更令人難以置信 。
i suspect we are now reaching the end of 400 years when western power was enough .	我懷疑我們現在要達到400年的終點 , 當西方權力足夠 。
people say to me , " the chinese , of course , they'll never get themselves involved in peacemaking , multilateral peacemaking around the world . "	人們對我說: 「 中國 , 當然 , 他們永遠不會自己參與和平、多種和平 , 世界各地的和平 。 」
oh yes ? why not ?	喔 , 是的 ? 為什麼不 ?
how many chinese troops are serving under the blue beret , serving under the blue flag , serving under the u . n . command in the world today ?	有多少中國軍隊在藍色的海底下服務 , 在藍色旗下服務 , 在聯合國的指揮下服務 ?
how many americans ? 11 .	有多少美國人 ? 11 。
what is the largest naval contingent tackling the issue of somali pirates ?	哪些是最大的罪犯 , 針對索馬利海盜的問題呢 ?
the chinese naval contingent .	中國航行的內容 。
of course they are , they are a mercantilist nation .	當然 , 他們是商業主義的國家 。
they want to keep the sea lanes open .	他們想要讓海車開放 。
increasingly , we are going to have to do business with people with whom we do not share values , but with whom , for the moment , we share common interests .	越來越多 , 我們將要和我們不共享價值的人做生意 , 但同時 , 對於當下 , 我們有共同利益 。
it's a whole new different way of looking at the world that is now emerging .	它是一個全新的看待世界的方式 。
and here's the third factor , which is totally different .	這是第三個因素 , 完全不同 。
today in our modern world , because of the internet , because of the kinds of things people have been talking about here , everything is connected to everything .	今天 , 在我們的現代世界 , 因為網路 , 因為人們在談論的事物 , 一切都與所有事物連結在一起 。
we are now interdependent .	我們現在是相互依賴的 。
we are now interlocked , as nations , as individuals , in a way which has never been the case before , never been the case before .	我們現在被關在 , 身為國家 , 身為個體 , 以以前從來沒有發生過的案例 。
the interrelationship of nations , well it's always existed .	國家的國際關係 , 總是存在的 。
diplomacy is about managing the interrelationship of nations .	外交是將國際國際的國際交互關注 。
but now we are intimately locked together .	但現在 , 我們終於被鎖在一起 。
you get swine flu in mexico , it's a problem for charles de gaulle airport 24 hours later .	你在墨西哥開啟了流感 , 它在24小時後就有一個問題 。
lehman brothers goes down , the whole lot collapses .	萊曼兄弟走下去 , 整個崩潰 。
there are fires in the steppes of russia , food riots in africa .	在俄羅斯的步驟中 , 糧食暴行 。
we are all now deeply , deeply , deeply interconnected .	我們現在都深深地 , 深深地連結在一起 。
and what that means is the idea of a nation state acting alone , not connected with others , not working with others , is no longer a viable proposition .	意思是 , 一個國家制度的概念 , 不是與其他人連結 , 而不是與其他人合作 , 不再是一個可見的建議 。
because the actions of a nation state are neither confined to itself , nor is it sufficient for the nation state itself to control its own territory , because the effects outside the nation state are now beginning to affect what happens inside them .	因為一個國家國家的行動也沒有限制自己 , 不論是國家制定自己的地位 , 要控制自己的地位 , 因為國家的效果開始影響到內在的情況 。
i was a young soldier in the last of the small empire wars of britain .	我是英國最後一個小帝國戰爭的年輕士兵 。
at that time , the defense of my country was about one thing and one thing only: how strong was our army , how strong was our air force , how strong was our navy and how strong were our allies .	那時 , 我國家的防禦是一件事 , 只有一件事:我們的軍隊有多強壯 , 我們的空軍有多強壯 , 我們的盟友有多強大 。
that was when the enemy was outside the walls .	那就是敵人在牆外 。
now the enemy is inside the walls .	敵人在牆裡 。
now if i want to talk about the defense of my country , i have to speak to the minister of health because pandemic disease is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of agriculture because food security is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of industry because the fragility of our hitech infrastructure is now a point of attack for our enemies as we see from cyber warfare i have to speak to the minister of home affairs because who has entered my country , who lives in that terraced house in that inner city has a direct effect on what happens in my country as we in london saw in the 7/7 bombings .	現在 , 如果我要談談我的國家防禦 , 我必須和健康部門談談 , 因為流行病對我的安全有威脅 , 我必須和農業總理談談談 , 因為食物安全是對我的安全感 , 我必須和產業的政黨談談 , 因為我們的希臘基礎建設 , 現在是我們在我們的敵人的攻擊 。
it's no longer the case that the security of a country is simply a matter for its soldiers and its ministry of defense .	它不再是國家安全的情況 , 只是對軍隊和其部門的重要性 。
it's its capacity to lock together its institutions .	它是它的能力 , 把其機構鎖在一起 。
and this tells you something very important .	這告訴你們一件非常重要的事 。
it tells you that , in fact , our governments , vertically constructed , constructed on the economic model of the industrial revolution vertical hierarchy , specialization of tasks , command structures have got the wrong structures completely .	它告訴各位 , 事實上 , 我們的政府 , 垂直建構了工業革命的經濟模式 , 建構在工業革命的經濟模式中 , 特殊的任務 , 指揮結構完全有錯誤的結構 。
you in business know that the paradigm structure of our time , ladies and gentlemen , is the network .	你在商業中知道 , 我們時代的範圍結構 , 先生女士們 , 是網路 。
it's your capacity to network that matters , both within your governments and externally .	這是你對網路的能力 , 在你的政府中 , 和外部都有 。
so here is ashdown's third law .	這裡是ashown第三法則 。
by the way , don't ask me about ashdown's first law and second law because i haven't invented those yet ; it always sounds better if there's a third law , doesn't it ?	順便說一提 , 別問我 , 阿什諾的第一法律和第二法律 , 因為我還沒發明這些 ; 如果有第三法律 , 聽起來更好嗎 ?
ashdown's third law is that in the modern age , where everything is connected to everything , the most important thing about what you can do is what you can do with others .	亞格蘭的第三法則是 , 在現代時代 , 每件事都與一切連結 , 最重要的是你能做的事是你能和其他人做的事 。
the most important bit about your structure whether you're a government , whether you're an army regiment , whether you're a business is your docking points , your interconnectors , your capacity to network with others .	最重要的是 , 你的結構不論是政府 , 不論你是軍隊監控 , 不論你是企業 , 你的內部人 , 你的能力和其他人的網路 。
you understand that in industry ; governments don't .	你知道在產業中 , 政府不會 。
but now one final thing .	但 , 最後一件事 。
if it is the case , ladies and gentlemen and it is that we are now locked together in a way that has never been quite the same before , then it's also the case that we share a destiny with each other .	如果是這個案例 , 先生女士們 , 我們現在被鎖在一個以前從來沒有相同的方式 , 那也是我們彼此共享的命運 。
suddenly and for the very first time , collective defense , the thing that has dominated us as the concept of securing our nations , is no longer enough .	突然間 , 一開始 , 集體防禦 , 把我們當作秘密我們的國家的概念 , 不再夠了 。
it used to be the case that if my tribe was more powerful than their tribe , i was safe ; if my country was more powerful than their country , i was safe ; my alliance , like nato , was more powerful than their alliance , i was safe .	以前 , 如果我的部落比他們的部落更強大 , 我很安全 ; 如果我的國家比他們的國家更加強大 ; 我的盟友 , 像是nato , 比他們的盟友更強大 , 我很安全 。
it is no longer the case .	它不再是這樣 。
the advent of the interconnectedness and of the weapons of mass destruction means that , increasingly , i share a destiny with my enemy .	大規模的破壞性和武器的進展 , 意味著 , 越來越多 , 我和敵人分享了一個命運 。
when i was a diplomat negotiating the disarmament treaties with the soviet union in geneva in the 1970s , we succeeded because we understood we shared a destiny with them .	當我還是一個外交官協商 , 和1970年代的蘇聯聯聯聯合在一起 , 我們成功了 , 因為我們知道我們和他們分享了命運 。
collective security is not enough .	集體安全不夠 。
peace has come to northern ireland because both sides realized that the zerosum game couldn't work .	和平來到北愛爾蘭 , 因為兩邊都意識到 , 零和遊戲無法運作 。
they shared a destiny with their enemies .	他們和他們的敵人分享了一個命運 。
one of the great barriers to peace in the middle east is that both sides , both israel and , i think , the palestinians , do not understand that they share a collective destiny .	中東的一個偉大的障礙是 , 以色列和平的兩邊 , 我想 , 巴勒斯坦人 , 不了解他們有共同的命運 。
and so suddenly , ladies and gentlemen , what has been the proposition of visionaries and poets down the ages becomes something we have to take seriously as a matter of public policy .	突然間 , 女士們先生們 , 正是視覺和詩人的建議 , 變成了我們必須認真的公共政策 。
i started with a poem , i'll end with one .	我從一首詩開始 , 最後會結束 。
the great poem of john donne's .	約翰•唐納的偉大詩 。
" send not for whom the bell tolls . "	「 不要為誰發送捐錢 。 」
the poem is called " no man is an island . "	詩叫做 「 沒有人是島嶼 」 。
and it goes: " every man's death affected me , for i am involved in mankind , send not to ask for whom the bell tolls , it tolls for thee . "	順便說: 「 每一位人的死亡都會影響我 , 我都參與了曼金 , 送不去詢問哪個貝殼 , 它會為此消失 。 」
for john donne , a recommendation of morality .	為約翰•唐諾尼 , 一個道德的建議 。
for us , i think , part of the equation for our survival .	對我們來說 , 我想 , 對我們的生存有一部分的方程式 。
to find the path to long life and health , dan buettner and team study the world's " blue zones , " communities whose elders live with vim and vigor to recordsetting age . at tedxtc , he shares the 9 common diet and lifestyle habits that keep them spry past age 100 .	為了找到長壽和健康的路徑 , 丹佛和團隊研究世界的 「 藍區 」 的 「 社區 」 和 「 受害者在tedxc 」 中 , 他分享了9個共同的飲食和生活習慣 , 讓它們傳達到100歲 。
biology , culture , exploration , food , health , life , science	生物學、文化、探索、食物、健康、生命、科學、科學、科學、生物、生物、生物、生物、生物、生物、生物、生物、生物、
dan buettner: how to live to be 100+	丹佛特:如何活到100+ 。
something called the danish twin study established that only about 10 percent of how long the average person lives , within certain biological limits , is dictated by our genes .	一個叫做丹麥雙胞胎的研究顯示 , 只有百分之十的平均人生活的壽命 , 在某些生物限制中 , 被我們的基因分歧 。
the other 90 percent is dictated by our lifestyle .	其他百分之九十的生命形式是被我們所影響的 。
so the premise of blue zones: if we can find the optimal lifestyle of longevity we can come up with a de facto formula for longevity .	所以 , 藍色區的前提:如果我們能找到長期壽的最佳生活方式 , 我們就能提出一個很長壽的公式 。
but if you ask the average american what the optimal formula of longevity is , they probably couldn't tell you .	但如果你問一般的美國人 , 長期的公式是什麼 , 他們可能不會告訴你 。
they've probably heard of the south beach diet , or the atkins diet .	他們可能聽過南海灘飲食 , 或皮膚的飲食 。
you have the usda food pyramid .	你有美國食物金字塔 。
there is what oprah tells us .	歐普拉告訴我們 。
there is what doctor oz tells us .	醫生奧茲告訴我們 。
the fact of the matter is there is a lot of confusion around what really helps us live longer better .	事實是 , 真正的幫助我們活得更久 。
should you be running marathons or doing yoga ?	你應該要跑馬拉松或做yoga ?
should you eat organic meats or should you be eating tofu ?	你應該要吃有機肉 , 或你應該吃湯匙嗎 ?
when it comes to supplements , should you be taking them ?	當它來到供應時 , 你應該把它們拿來嗎 ?
how about these hormones or resveratrol ?	那麼 , 這些荷爾蒙或逆轉器呢 ?
and does purpose play into it ?	純粹的玩樂是嗎 ?
spirituality ? and how about how we socialize ?	精神性 ? 以及我們如何社交呢 ?
well , our approach to finding longevity was to team up with national geographic , and the national institute on aging , to find the four demographically confirmed areas that are geographically defined .	我們找到長期的研究方法 , 就是和國家地理學合作 , 而國家的研究研究 , 尋找四個人口 , 確認地理定義的區域 。
and then bring a team of experts in there to methodically go through exactly what these people do , to distill down the crosscultural distillation .	接著 , 把專家的團隊帶進去 , 以準確地通過這些人所做的事 , 來分解跨越文化歧視 。
and at the end of this i'm going to tell you what that distillation is .	最後 , 我要告訴你們這一點點是什麼 。
but first i'd like to debunk some common myths when it comes to longevity .	但首先 , 我想在長期來看一些常見的迷思 。
and the first myth is if you try really hard you can live to be 100 .	第一個迷思是 , 如果你真的很難活到100歲 。
the problem is , only about one out of 5 , 000 people in america live to be 100 .	問題是 , 美國只有5 , 000人住在一百人 。
your chances are very low .	你的機會很低 。
even though it's the fastest growing demographic in america , it's hard to reach 100 .	儘管它是美國最快速成長的人口數位 , 很難達到100 。
the problem is that we're not programmed for longevity .	問題是 , 我們不是為了長壽的程式 。
we are programmed for something called procreative success .	我們為一個叫做 「 成功成功 」 的程式編碼 。
i love that word .	我喜歡這個詞 。
it reminds me of my college days .	它提醒我大學的日子 。
biologists term procreative success to mean the age where you have children and then another generation , the age when your children have children .	生物學家認為有孩子和其他世代的成功 , 隨著孩子有孩子的年齡 , 孩子有孩子的年齡 。
after that the effect of evolution completely dissipates .	演化的效果完全不適用 。
if you're a mammal , if you're a rat or an elephant , or a human , in between , it's the same story .	如果你是個哺乳類動物 , 如果你是老鼠或大象 , 或人類 , 兩者之間 , 它是相同的 。
