so if this was happening , your memories could start by place cells activating each other via these dense interconnections and then reactivating boundary cells to create the spatial structure of the scene around your viewpoint .	所以 , 如果這發生了 , 你的記憶可以從細胞開始 , 讓彼此活化 , 維持這些密度的連結 , 然後反應邊界細胞 , 來創造你的觀點的空間結構 。
and grid cells could move this viewpoint through that space .	網格細胞可以透過這個空間移動這個觀點 。
another kind of cell , head direction cells , which i didn't mention yet , they fire like a compass according to which way you're facing .	另外一種細胞 , 頭部 , 我還沒提到的細胞 , 它們會像同情的同情 , 例如你所面對的方式 。
they could define the viewing direction from which you want to generate an image for your visual imagery , so you can imagine what happened when you were at this wedding , for example .	他們可以定義你想要為你的視覺影像創造一個影像 , 所以你可以想像當你在婚禮上發生了什麼事 。
so this is just one example of a new era really in cognitive neuroscience where we're beginning to understand psychological processes like how you remember or imagine or even think in terms of the actions of the billions of individual neurons that make up our brains .	這只是一個新時代的一個例子 , 真正是認知神經科學 , 我們開始了解心理過程 , 例如你如何記憶或想像 , 甚至認為數十億個個人神經元的動作 。
thank you very much .	非常謝謝大家 。
imagine a global security driven by collaboration among agencies , government , the private sector and the public . that's not just the distant hope of opensource fans , it's the vision of james stavridis , the supreme commander of nato , who shares vivid moments from recent military history to explain why security of the future should be built with bridges rather than walls .	想像一個全球安全驅使在機構中合作 , 政府 , 私人部門和公共場所 。 這不僅是開放資源掃描的遠景 , 也是最高的俄羅斯總署 , 來自近期的軍事歷史 , 來解釋未來的安全性 。
collaboration , global issues , opensource , peace , politics , social media , violence , war	合作、全球議題、開放資源、和平、政治、社交媒體、暴力、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、全球議題、開放、開放、和平、和平、和平、政治、社會媒體、社會媒體、暴力、暴力
james stavridis: how nato's supreme commander thinks about global security	詹姆斯•史里迪:娜托的最高指揮官認為全球安全安全性是怎樣的 。
i'm gonna talk a little bit about opensource security , because we've got to get better at security in this 21st century .	我想要談的是開放資源安全 , 因為我們必須在21世紀得到更好的安全性 。
let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	首先 , 咱們回顧二十世紀 , 了解安全方式對我們來說是如何運作的 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是fdun , 在法國的北方 , 一場戰鬥 , 僅僅是海軍總部的北部 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	1916年 , 超過300000年的人死亡 , 大約有70萬人死亡 , 大約有2千人一天 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	假如你將它推進第二次世界大戰中 , 你看到史達丁文的戰鬥 , 三百天 , 殺死了 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們走進冷戰 , 我們繼續嘗試建造牆壁 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從第一次世界大戰到第二次世界大戰 , 然後我們進入冷戰、鐵牆、柏林牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	今天我的論點是 , 不是建築牆來創造安全 , 我們需要建立橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲有名的橋 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它是華盛頓河的橋樑 , 由ivoandroandri的小說主題 , 談到歐洲和巴爾克人的一部分 , 經過了很大的牆壁 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	最近 , 在過去的十年裡 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 致力於聚集在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我再次爭論 , 開放資源安全是關聯國際 , 內部的介面 , 私人的矛盾 , 將它與策略溝通 , 大多在社交網路上 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	讓我來談談為什麼我們要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球共同點在各種方式下攻擊 , 沒有任何威脅來源 , 都可以用建牆來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	很顯然 , 我是一名sailor ,
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一條線 , 穿過印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片中有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	它的邊部有了音樂會線 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	那就是防止海盜攻擊它 。
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	piracy今天是世界上非常活躍的威脅 。 這是印度的海洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	piracy也非常活躍在馬拉克卡的時代 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	在幾內亞灣 , 它是活躍的 。
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海看到它 。
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	它是全球運輸系統中的10億美金的距離 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 在那裡 , 有20個船長 , 500名馬丁人被告住了 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是全球共同點的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要思考如何解決它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉換到不同的海洋 , 網路海 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這是兩個年輕人的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	那時 , 他們被監禁了 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們做了一個信用卡片 , 把它們連上一百億美金 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 是全球經濟的2兆美金 。
two trillion a year .	每年有2兆美元 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	這只是在英國的gdp上 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以 , 這種網路海 , 我們無盡地知道 , 是最根本的開放性 , 也是威脅的 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	另一個我擔心全球共同點的威脅是被販賣的威脅 , 由奈米生物、鴉片般的運動 , 來自歐洲的阿富汗 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心 , 來自安東北的古柯鹼 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的動作和交易 。 最重要的是 , 或許 , 我們擔心人類販賣 , 和它的成本很糟糕 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	販賣大多在海中移動 , 但在全球共同點的其他部分 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你們 , 這是個非常高科技的傢伙 , 我們使用的是停止販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是用藥物卡爾來進行的半米麻煩 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	它是由南美的叢林組成 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那個低科技的雷射捕捉它 , 牠會帶著六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個 , 複雜的溝通 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	在人類、武器、上帝禁止 , 在大規模破壞的武器中 , 是全球共同的威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	今天我們把它拉到阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是阿富汗的最快樂領域 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上有8%到90%的貧窮、鴉片和海洛因 , 來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	我們也看到 , 當然 , 恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是蓋達組織的位置 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個非常強烈的急診所 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義也是全球共同點的一部分 , 我們必須解決問題 。
so here we are , 21st century .	這裡是21世紀 。
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們的20世紀工具不會成功 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我會爭論 , 我們不會從一個槍枝的障礙來傳遞安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會從槍枝的桶子裡傳送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們會需要軍方力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這麼做時 , 我們一定要做得很好 , 競爭 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放資源安全是關於國際、介入、私人的聯繫 , 由網路上的策略溝通的想法 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我給你們幾個例子 , 說明一下 , 這怎麼做是正面的 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都在包住書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 那很奇怪 , 我想我在20歲和30歲的年輕男性和女性 , 大部分都是阿富汗的幻覺 。 」
you would be correct .	你會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全力量時 , 85%無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班在這些男人和女性學會如何閱讀時期時 , 她們會學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以 , 問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們閱讀文學課程 , 透過私人部門和開發機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過二十萬名阿富汗安全部隊去閱讀和寫下基本的程度 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你可以在阿富汗讀書時 , 你通常會把筆放在你的口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	當這些年輕男性和女性畢業時 , 他們會拿這筆錢 , 放進他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這將國際聯合在一起 , 有五十個國家參與這個任務 , 這些發展機構 , 私人共和黨 , 來取得這種安全性 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們戰鬥技巧 , 但是我會爭論 , 開放資源安全的意義 , 意味著建立更久的安全效應 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國航海軍 。
it's called the comfort .	它叫做舒適 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一個姐妹船叫 「 商業 」 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院船 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這首歌 , 舒適 , 透過加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的危機上 , 他們會做四十萬個病人治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它不是因為軍方而被人道主義組織的結合:操作希望、專案微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織會發送志願者 。
interagency physicians come out .	介入醫師出席了 。
they're all part of this .	他們都是這樣的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	為各位舉一個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他媽媽兩天走上眼睛診所 , 以舒適的方式來實現 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被騙了 , 他的雙眼時 , 他突然想到 , 說: 「 媽媽 , 維多多•里奧 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽 , 我看到世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	多次以40萬的病人治療 , 這種私人的共和黨合作 , 你開始看到創造安全的力量 , 以非常不同的方式創造安全 。
here you see baseball players .	在這裡 , 你看到棒球玩家 。
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能否挑出這張照片中的兩個美國軍隊嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這些年輕男孩的兩個年輕人 。 這是一系列的鹼基診所的一部分 , 我們探討了大型的同事balleball的合作 , 國際軍隊的軍隊 , 軍事棒球玩家 , 他們是真正的技巧 , 但參與了這段旅程中 , 他們在拉丁美洲和加州的巴勒比亞州 , 全國各地的巴勒斯加州 , 全國的巴勒比亞 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它給年輕男性和女性的角色 , 展現了社會的角色 , 以及關於我爭議的生命 , 幫助我們為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這夥伴的另一面是災難的宗教 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍直升機 , 在2004年海嘯 , 殺死了25萬人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些大災難中 , 2004年的海嘯 , 2004年 , 25萬人死於巴基斯坦 , 2005 , 8萬人死於海地地震 , 大約有30萬人死了 , 近來是最糟糕的地震組合 , 而核產業的產業 , 在這些產業中 , 我們看到了國際性行業 , 和國際性行業之間的關係 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些是開放資源安全的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們不斷地把它綁在一起 , 藉由做類似的事情 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你在看這個想法: 「 啊 , 阿米蘭 , 這些必須是通訊的海道 , 或這些可能是纖維的電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 , 這是全球推特的圖表 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫外線是推文 。 綠色是地理 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是一個完美的演說 , 偉大的人口調查 , 世界上有六大的國家在描述秩序:中國、印度、臉書、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們要在這些垃圾裡 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前談到阿拉伯的春天 , 和這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我會給你另一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表了一陣子的演講 。 我說 , 正如我對你們所有人說的 , 我在臉書 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽眾聽起來有點笑 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章 , 由ap跑到電線上 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	在世界上有兩個地方 , 芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	頭條是:娜托需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 第二天早上 , 我有數百位臉書朋友 , 來自印尼人和芬蘭 , 大部分的說: 「 阿米蘭人 , 我們聽過你需要朋友 , 喔 , 喔 , 俄羅斯是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動這個訊息 , 傳遞訊息是我們如何連結國際 , 介入、私人的國際網路 , 這些社交網 , 協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我來打個十一月的音 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張很勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭警衛中 。
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在高爾蘭 , 位在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡提醒我們 , 我不希望任何人離開房間思考 , 我們不需要有能力、競爭的軍隊才能創造真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這是我們所做的核心和我們所做的 , 來保護自由、自由、言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍惜的事物 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道的 , 生命不是一場開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有很困難的戰役 , 或在巴克的戰鬥中 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會爭論生命是旋轉的 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須把它放進去 , 正如我在21世紀 , 我們將如何在真正的戰爭和危機上產生安全感 , 但現在 , 我們的軍隊能夠創造出21世紀的安全、國際關係、私人的溝通 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我會說 , 我們今天早就聽過維基百科 。 我隨時都用維基百科來查看事實 , 維基百科並不是在一個房間中鎖定的文章中 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天 , 有數萬人輸入資訊 , 每一天 , 數百萬人在做這些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	對於基本的點子來說 , 一個完美的圖像 , 沒有人會像我們一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有人 , 沒有一個人盟友 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有人跟我們一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的視覺表達非常簡單:一個世界 , 每個人都能自由分享所有知識的總和 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 結合國際、介入、私人、策略溝通 , 在21世紀 , 我們可以創造所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常謝謝你 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
